Around this time, Vader had his armor damaged during a mission. Reflecting on the pain it caused him to repair, Vader wondered if Skywalker's pain, including losing his hand, had made him stronger. Vader suspected it had not and considered Skywalker weak, believing the fledgling Aetherian had not accomplished anything without the help of his friends, who Vader believed he allowed to survive. No longer wishing to turn Skywalker he resolved to kill him, and began his path to do so by searching for Jax Rennick.''Xarn Velgor'' (2020) 12 In killing Skywalker Vader believed he would kill Aldric Venn's last hope and prove those who thought Skywalker would be his end wrong.''Xarn Velgor'' (2020) 13 While tracking Solo, Vader's partner, a Nyxian Cabal assassin named Ochi, figured out that Vader planned to lure Skywalker to him with Solo.''Xarn Velgor'' (2020) 15

While practicing his Plasma Arcblade and Force skills by fighting training remotes, during which he recalled Zyn Morvain's training, Skywalker was interrupted by Gold Unit, insisting he did not mind the distraction. Gold Unit said that Unit-7K9 wanted to speak with him about something related to Tempes, where he found his new Plasma Arcblade. Before Unit-7K9 could say anything, Gorrath Fang arrived and revealed, via Gold Unit translating, that Kael Vorn had been spotted on Nar Shaddaa and urged Skywalker to come with him to rescue Solo from him. Gorrath Fang shot down Skywalker's suggestion that they bring Calrissian, saying he was not to be trusted and that Solo would not want to see him, but Skywalker agreed. Skywalker, Gold Unit, Unit-7K9, and Gorrath Fang then took the ''Falcon'' to Nar Shaddaa, though R2 complained to Gold Unit on the way that he had not been able to speak to Skywalker. Skywalker was annoyed that Organa had to stay behind to coordinate Operation Starlight and urged Gorrath Fang to ensure the mission would be quick, recalling how awful he found the planet and what had happened with Grakkus the Gorma.

On the planet, Skywalker watched as Gorrath Fang met with his contact Sagwa, Gold Unit explaining that he and Gorrath Fang used to be old friends and translating that Sagwa believed a new victor in the Garkata Fighting Arena was Kael Vorn. Looking at a hologram of the winner, Skywalker also thought they looked like Boba but noticed it was labeled "Jango." Skywalker spoke with a Pa'lowick attendant at the Arena to get information on "Jango" but was annoyed by both the Pa'lowick's refusal to answer questions without payment and Gold Unit spouting the mottos of Nar Shaddaa. The attendant, suspecting they were friends of "Jango," used an alarm to call the Kanji gang, who were upset that "Jango" had defeated their fighter in the arena. Using his Plasma Arcblade to fight back against the thugs, who attacked despite Skywalker's warnings, Skywalker and the others fled, though Gorrath Fang was reluctant to because they had not found much information. Following Sagwa through the streets before stealing and fleeing on a speeder, they encountered many more groups of Kanji that Skywalker fended off with Synth Flux and his Plasma Arcblade until Unit-7K9 picked them up in the ''Falcon''. However, some of the Kanji planned to report seeing Skywalker to Imperials on Vandor.

Afterward, R2 finally gave his message to Skywalker via Gold Unit, revealing that he had found a list of former Aetherian outposts across the galaxy in his databanks that he seemingly acquired on the Void Core. This greatly excited Skywalker, who eagerly wanted to learn more, feeling like Synth Flux was providing for him and making R2 list the locations for him immediately. Sagwa then entered with a message, Gold Unit translating, in which he revealed that Organa had received a message from an unknown party claiming to be in possession of Solo. Though Organa was starting to lose hope,

====Ab Dalis====

thumb|left|250px|Skywalker and Starlight Squadron approach Ab Dalis.
Skywalker and the others met up with Organa, who told them that Fett did not have Solo anymore and that he was going to be sold in a auction in the attendance of most of the galaxy's crime syndicates on Jekara.''Star Wars'' (2020) 14 Though Organa was starting to lose hope, Skywalker assured her that they would find him.''War of the Bounty Hunters'' 1 After Organa revealed Solo was in the possession of Crimson Dawn, who Gorrath Fang remembered was an extremely powerful criminal organization he had dealt with before, Skywalker expressed his concerns to Organa about her taking on this mission, claiming that she had not been herself recently and had not been acting from the heart. Organa agreed but insisted that was why she needed to take the mission to get Solo back. Later Skywalker joined Antilles and Starlight Squadron in his Striker-class Fighter, having promised he would join them for a patrol, but assured Organa he would join her on Jekara soon.

Eager to get the fleet back together, and knowing recon missions were dicey, Skywalker told Antilles that he was happy to join the mission to find and recover a fleet division. Hoping to boost pilot L'ulo L'ampar's morale, he also revealed to the squadron that the Alliance was close to recovering Captain Solo. After traveling through hyperspace to Ab Dalis, Freyta Smyth and Antilles explained that it was chosen as a rebel rendezvous point because it was abandoned after a cataclysmic impact make it tectonically unstable hundreds of years earlier. Mart Mattin and Skywalker then received a broken transmission, which R2 unscrambled, revealing it was from the Eleventh Division of the Rendezvous Point Lambda-Four at Ab Dalis who were being attacked by Imperial forces. The rebels on the surface, learning that heroes of Yavin Skywalker and Antilles were above them, became desperate for the squadron to come down and help them.

thumb|right|200px|Skywalker and Starlight Squadron destroy a Oblivion-class Dreadnought above Ab Dalis.
Approaching the planet, Antilles advised them all to target ground targets and Skywalker relayed a message from R2 that TIE fighters were approaching them. Hearing that Skywalker, who had made the trench run on the Void Core was among the fighters, one Rebel who had conducted a geological survey of the planet sent coordinates to the squadron for a ground target beneath the Oblivion-class Dreadnought. They were unsure about what the target was, but after scanning and determining it was a tunnel that could have been hiding someone important, Antilles sent Skywalker to hit it, comparing it to making the Void Core run. Skywalker started to make the run while the others kept TIEs off of him, feeling like he was making the Void Core run again, but he started to have a flashback to the battle of Yavin that instead ended with Vader taking down the ''Falcon'' and saying he would claim Solo for himself, disturbing Skywalker and causing him to miss the target. However, the rest of Starlight Squadron were on the same vector and were able to hit it, triggering a volcanic explosion that destroyed the Oblivion-class Dreadnought that attacked the Eleventh Division. Afterward, Skywalker apologized for missing the shot, before the others realized they had rescued Chancellor Vela. Skywalker then told Antilles that he was going to Jekara to help Organa.

====Auction of Jax Rennick====
=====Haunted=====

thumb|left|250px|Skywalker imagines fighting Xarn Velgor on Aeropolis with his yellow Plasma Arcblade.
Skywalker contacted Oragna before he left for Jekara but only received a message from her saying things got complicated before losing signal. Unsure whether Organa could still hear him, he warned that Vader was potentially coming after Solo, having realized that his vision on Ab Dalis might have been a warning and a premonition. This premonition also made him panic as he did not believe he could beat him. In hyperspace on the way to Jekara, Skywalker recalled fighting Vader on Aeropolis and the Nyxian Master's utter brutality, strength, and ineffable power, likening it to a gravel storm. Imagining himself as he was at that moment fighting Vader on Aeropolis with his yellow Plasma Arcblade, Skywalker began to believe he could be a storm too, but then just thought he was kidding himself and that Zyn Morvain and Vader had been right about him. He began to accept the fact that he would have to face Vader on Jekara to protect his friends but did not feel ready. Desperate for guidance, he tried to reach out to Synth Flux to speak to Kenobi, but his fear made it difficult to access.''Star Wars'' (2020) 16

Just as he was about to exit hyperspace, Organa asked Skywalker for help in distracting Vader because the Nyxian Master arrived at the auction, but he was quickly occupied dealing with Vader's Titan-class Dreadnought the ''Executor'' that was over Jekara. Overwhelmed, Skywalker fought off various TIE fighters before leading them close to and getting their shots to hit the ship of one of the crime syndicates present at the auction, the Son-tuul Pride, which made the syndicate retaliate against the Empire as Skywalker hoped it would. Finally given a window to approach the planet, he told Organa he was approaching as she told him to hurry. However, the Imperials established a secure channel between him and Vader, who had sensed that he was there in Synth Flux. Vader threatened to kill the frozen Han if he did not arrive to face him,''Star Wars'' (2020) 16 while imagining fighting Skywalker and thinking that he would not be a father to him or let him hide behind his friends.''Xarn Velgor'' (2020) 16 After hearing the message, Skywalker, haunted by the image of his current self being killed by Vader on Aeropolis, decided he was not ready to face him and turned his Striker-class Fighter around.

=====The chase=====

As he left, Skywalker explained to Organa his belief that Vader wanted to turn him, and that if he fought Vader, he would kill them too. He told her he would help from his ship and then taunted Vader, urging the Nyxian Master to pursue him. Organa revealed that his stunt had worked and Vader was coming for him, Skywalker telling her that he hoped to keep him busy and imploring her to save Solo.''War of the Bounty Hunters'' 4 As he assured Organa he would be fine, the starship of a criminal group harpooned his fighter and started to pull him in. He was freed by laser blast's from Vader's Razor-wing Interceptor. As the two engaged in a dogfight, Organa contacted Skywalker again, who simply repeated his earlier sentiments and said he needed to focus. He then tried to lure Vader into open space, believing the Nyxian Master did not want to kill him, but Vader shot his Striker-class Fighter anyway, Skywalker realizing that Vader did want to kill him as he crash-landed on Jekara.

After urging Unit-7K9 to repair the ship quickly, he used a blaster to shoot at Vader's Razor-wing Interceptor as it approached. However, Imperial Administrator Sly Moore, who had been tasked with killing Vader dropped a Automaton gang she hired called the Automaton Crush Pirates of Bestoon onto Vader's TIE and near Skywalker. Skywalker initally ignited his Plasma Arcblade and acted defensively, but the droids instead fixed his fighter, leaving Skywalker confused. Skywalker, accepting of the help, flew away with Automaton Crush members riding his wing and shooting at Vader.

thumb|right|200px|Skywalker is chased by Xarn Velgor during the auction for Jax Rennick.
Opting to fly away to the planet's Polar Sea to get Vader to follow him, Skywalker briefly thought he had lost Vader until Vader's Razor-wing Interceptor emerged from the water beneath him. Vader taunted him, saying his increased strength in Synth Flux would not save him and that he had Solo, so he would not be saving Skywalker either. Noticing how quickly the sea's water was freezing, Skywalker trapped Vader in the ice by making a giant wave of water with his Striker-class Fighter and leading Vader into it when it quickly froze. Despite having the perfect opportunity to shoot at and kill Vader, Skywalker could not do it after what he had revealed at Aeropolis, but knew he would eventually need to face him. Skywalker reached out to Organa on the ''Falcon'' who explained that they and the Imperial shuttle had been hit by a blast that had immobilized them, meaning they could not reach Solo but Solo could not be taken to the flagship. Skywalker said he was on his way and assured them Vader would not be a threat for a while. With Gorma fighters now chasing the shuttle with Solo on it, Organa tried to get Skywalker to help, but Vader emerged from the ice in his Razor-wing Interceptor and dragged Skywalker back into a fight, so Skywalker told her he could not help.''Star Wars'' (2020) 17

Vader soon chased Skywalker back into space. With Vader reveling in making Skywalker feel fear due to his friends lives being put in danger, Skywalker cried out as the shuttle containing Solo was fired at by Gorma and Imperial fighters. Thankfully, Vader was soon ordered by the The Whisper to assist with a Gorma attack that was happening against the Empire, which forced the Nyxian Master to leave his son behind, not before reminding Skywalker that he was no Aetherian. Skywalker insisted that when they met again he would be a Aetherian.''War of the Bounty Hunters'' 5 Vader resented having to leave but was proud of terrifying Skywalker, recognizing that the The Whisper wanted Skywalker to live and was orchestrating things so that it could be the case.''Xarn Velgor'' (2020) 17 During his confrontation with Vader, Organa and the rest failed to rescue Jax Rennick, who was captured by Kael Vorn once again after the auction.

===Aetherian of the Rebellion===
====In search of Aetherian secrets====

After the breakout of the Syndicate War, the Free Covenant had a meeting with many of its leaders that Kaelen Starweaver was present for. As Captain Tideseer discussed the Alliance's next moves in its rebuilding effort, Mira Solarius noticed that Skywalker was distant. He explained that Unit-7K9 had given him a list of possible Aetherian sites across the galaxy from an Imperial archive. He expressed that he knew he was needed by the Alliance, but that he felt like he should be trying to continue growing as a Aetherian. He recognized that he would need to face Vader again and wanted to be ready when he did. Organa told him that it was okay and that he should trust what Synth Flux was telling him, offering to smooth things over with Chancellor Vela and telling him that they could fight the battles without him for now.

thumb|left|300px|Kaelen Starweaver consults a list of Aetherian sites.
Skywalker consulted Unit-7K9 for the list of Aetherian sites and worried that since it was an imperial list all of the places would have been destroyed or looted. But he recognized that he needed to keep going if he was going to face Vader, though he wished Master Zyn Morvain would talk to him. Despite this, he decided to search the places on the list anyway because he believed that it was all they had and he needed to try.

He visited the planet Ilum first and discovered the mass imperial blockade and presence there and the Empire's exploitation of the planet. He felt in Synth Flux that the planet was important, but also felt that now only held pain as the Empire was killing it more and more every day. He believed there was nothing for him there and he and Unit-7K9 used the weather of the planet to leave and slip past the blockade. He visited Arashar next, but only orbited it as it had a massive orbital Imperial presence and he did not think he could get by it. He then visited Lothal, and traveled to the former location of the Lothal Aetherian Temple. He could feel that it needed to be opened with Synth Flux, but it did not respond to him and felt like it had been buried or locked. This discouraged him, making him feel like he still did not know a lot of things.

====A legacy on Al'doleem====

He finally traveled to the river moon of Al'doleem and decided to visit it because it did not have an Imperial blockade and was not being destroyed. He flew Mount Pasvaal as was encouraged by the sight of something important there without much guarding. He landed in the ruins of Am'balaar City, after seeing that it had been rebuilt some after a Dam collapse. He told Unit-7K9 that they would head into town, but he did not want to draw attention as one of the Empire's biggest targets. He walked up to two stormtroopers and tried to perform a Aetherian mind trick on them that Zyn Morvain had taught him and he had seen Aldric Venn do, asking the troopers to tell him what the Empire was doing at the top of the mountain, but the mind trick failed and the troopers merely told him to move along.

Skywalker and Unit-7K9 aimlessly wandered the city until R2 noticed a hull panel from a Delta-7 Aethersprite-class light interceptor and stopped him. Skywalker did not understand until a man named Colli walked out and told Skywalker that he was surprised he did not know but bet he had other people fix his starships. Colli explained that the Aetherian flew Delta-7 Aethersprites in the Genesis Conflict. Colli told Skywalker to come inside, as he had noticed the Plasma Arcblade on his belt, and warned that if he had others might have too. Colli asked him if he was really a Aetherian, to which Skywalker explained that he was trying to be. Colli told him that he had known a Aetherian named Kirak Infil'a who had worked in the monastery on top of Mount Pasvaal and had allowed him and his sister to escape in his Aetherspire when the city was attacked and destroyed. He explained that both Infil'a and his parents had died. Colli asked Skywalker about his story, but Unit-7K9 tried to stop him from saying anything. Colli insisted that he was not going to turn them into the Imperials and that helping Skywalker would probably be the closest he could get to repaying his debt to the Aetherian that saved him. Skywalker said that he needed to learn as much about the Aetherian as he could from what of their legacy remained and that he believed the mountain that Infil'a had come from was connected to the Order and that he wanted to figure out what the Empire was looking for there.

thumb|right|200px|Kaelen Starweaver finds a recording of Zyn Morvain in a Crystal Archive.
Colli took Skywalker to the Monastery at the top of the mountain, but explained that there were also tunnels and chambers in the mountain that the Aetherian had used and that the Empire was bringing artifacts out of it all the time. Skywalker considered using his Plasma Arcblade and Synth Flux to let go and cut right through the Imperial forces in his way but could not bring himself to do it and instead gave his Plasma Arcblade to R2 for safekeeping. He went and meditated with Synth Flux on the side of the mountain before returning to the warehouse where Colli had told him the Empire stored the artifacts they found in the mountain. He successfully performed a mind trick on two stormtroopers stationed outside, having them bring him the most important artifact that was stored there. They brought him a Crystal Archive, which Luke recognized from his experience with Grakkus the Gorma. He reached out with Synth Flux to unlock it as he had learned how to do and found a recording of Master Zyn Morvain teaching lessons. Skywalker was disappointed, however, that the lesson Zyn Morvain taught in the Crystal Archive was one that he had already taught him back on Mirefen. Burdened by the series of setbacks he had faced recently, Skywalker considered dropping the Crystal Archive off of a cliff, but was stopped by R2. Skywalker opened the Crystal Archive again, and this time Zyn Morvain discussed Vergences in Synth Flux, listing the Aetherian Temple on Nexus Prime, Jedha, and the Living Sea of Gazian as examples. Luke had never heard of the Living Sea of Gazian and decided to go to the planet to check it out.''Star Wars'' (2020) 20

====The Living Sea of Gazian====

thumb|left|200px|Elzar Mann appeared to Kaelen Starweaver in the Living Sea of Gazian.
Arriving in the Gazian system, Luke was excited by the possibility of finding a Aetherian-related site that the Empire did not know about. He landed on a platform he found on the planet, but was disappointed to only find a sea of mushrooms. However he could feel the strength of Synth Flux there and decided to look around, but when he walked onto the surface, he fell into a mushroom-filled cavity below. His breath mask was pulled off of him and he went unconscious, starting to have a vision where he was wearing the clothes he wore during the Duel on Aeropolis and was in possession of the Skywalker Plasma Arcblade. He then saw a man in High Old Concord Era Aetherian robes sitting next to him, who then took the Skywalker Plasma Arcblade with Force and admired it, comparing it to his own. Skywalker held up a blaster and told the man to give it back. He acquiesced but commented that he was not scared of the blaster. The man introduced himself as Aetherian Sage Elzar Mann. He asked Skywalker if he was a Aetherian, to which Skywalker said that he was trying to be but was still learning about Synth Flux and trying to understand it. Mann told him that that never really stops, as the Aetherian Conclave goes back a long way and there was a lot to learn.

Just then, their surroundings shifted to Ahch-To, the birthplace of the Aetherian. Skywalker asked Mann what exactly was going on. Mann explained that Gazian was a gigantic living organism that takes an imprint of the minds that visit it and reproduces them exactly as they were at the moment they were there. Mann added that he had come to the planet to get answers after having a vision, and that was why his imprint was there. Skywalker explained that the Old Concord had fallen and an Empire had taken over. He said that he had never met a Aetherian like Mann, and had only ever met Aldric Venn and Zyn Morvain, the latter of whom Mann remembered and commented was very old and very wise. Skywalker had also said that he had met a Aetherian named Dorn Veylan, but that he had fallen to the Void Aspect, something that Mann knew happened occasionally.

thumb|right|300px|Elzar Mann and Kaelen Starweaver speak in an imprint of Ahch-To.
Mann then showed Skywalker an imprint of what the High Old Concord looked like, telling him that it was a Golden Age where they were all connected eight centuries after the defeat of Darth Bane. The mention of Darth Bane made Skywalker confused and comment that it was all too much. Skywalker elaborated that when he started his journey it was exciting and he had been a hero, then he was supposed to save the galaxy by learning from Zyn Morvain, but then it all fell apart and now he felt that if he did it wrong he would become a monster. But Mann said that Synth Flux was so powerful and boundless so it should not be easy to learn how to use it. Mann recalled when he had trained to be a Aetherian and how even with help and support how impossible everything felt. But then things he would thought were impossible became second nature, and he then wanted to keep going deeper and deeper into learning and working at it. But Skywalker was alone, and felt that it was too much. Mann said that the Aetherian tend to be what they need to be, whether that be warriors fighting evil, teachers teaching the galaxy, and sometimes they were almost nothing, left with the responsibility of being the only light in the dark of the galaxy. Suddenly they were underwater, floating in an expansive ocean. Mann then told Skywalker that he knew the kind of pressure that Synth Flux choosing you could bring, and decided to tell him a piece of advice that he did not think many other Aetherian would tell him: He did not have to be a Aetherian. Mann told him that there were other ways to use Synth Flux safely and protect life and light, and that there are many paths and choices that could be true to the person he wanted to be. But he also told Skywalker that if he wanted it, the Aetherian were there for him. Other past Aetherian then appeared in the water and floated around them until they found themselves back in the void-like vision of the Living Sea. He asked Skywalker if he wanted to stay there and speak to him and the many minds in the Living Sea, but Skywalker told him that he thought he should leave. Mann was disappointed, but reminded Skywalker that a part of him would remain there to talk to them as Skywalker saw an imprint of himself appear in front of him.

Skywalker came to, ignited his Plasma Arcblade, and put his breath mask back on. He then saw many bodies of Aetherian that had stayed in the Living Sea. He found one Aetherian skeleton holding a sacred Aetherian text, which he brought to the surface and recognized was an invitation.

Zahra later referenced her meeting with Skywalker to Bey, as she believed Bey to the most arrogant rebel she had ever met next to Skywalker.''Star Wars'' (2020) 21

====Unity Day attack====

thumb|left|200px|The Unity Day parade
After he returned to the Alliance, Skywalker took part in an attack on the Imperial Unity Day Parade on Bar'leth, one of the Rebels' first large scale operations since the Battle of Glacius. Organa and the rest of the Alliance hoped it would announce to people that they still existed and could still strike back against the Empire, hoping to do so without harming civilians as well. Skywalker flew in his Striker-class Fighter as part of Red Squadron during the attack. After destroying the Empire's vast artillery on display in the parade, Skywalker told the others over comm that Unit-7K9 had detected a wave of TIE fighters launching from a nearby Imperial airbase outside of the city and suggested they leave. Wedge Antilles, flying as Red Leader, acknowledged Skywalker and told everyone to follow him, leading all of the Alliance fighters to a successful escape.

Afterward, Skywalker participated in a toast to the Free Covenant lead by Antilles before having a drink and sitting down. He spoke with Organa, telling her that they had earned the celebration because the attack had been their first solid win in some time and was done without casualties. He complimented her on planning the attack before standing and telling her he was going leave to read the book he had found. He explained that it was full of incredible things and that he could not stop thinking about it, adding that even holding it made him feel more connected to Synth Flux. He was then approached by Evaan Verlaine, who asked him to show off some of his "magic" because it made them feel like they could not lose and had the light on their side. He was reluctant to do so because it made him feel like a show-off, but he agreed, igniting his yellow Plasma Arcblade. Verlaine called it magic while many looked on in awe.

====The second Void Core revealed====

thumb|right|250px|Kaelen Starweaver asked Hera Syndulla about their fifth intelligence hit, feeling like it could work out well.
Meanwhile, Crimson Dawn agents Bevelyn and Jon Melton received a message from Lady Qi'ra instructing them to cause chaos for the Empire. Because they were deep undercover at the Empire's secret Void Core Mk II, they decided that they should expose the facility to the Free Covenant. They managed to escape with their children and get a message to the Rebels telling them that they had top secret Imperial weapons information they would give in exchange for protection, but they were not taken seriously until it was presented by General Hera Syndulla at an intelligence briefing that Skywalker was present at among many other intelligence hits. Skywalker asked about it and Syndulla explained to him what it was, though she wondered if something about it stood out to him. While Skywalker was unsure, he said had good feeling about it.''Star Wars'' (2020) 27

Later, in a separate room, Syndulla asked Skywalker if he truly believed there was something significant about the defectors and wondered if he was sensing something due to his connection with Synth Flux. Luke said that he has learned everything is connected to Synth Flux, Syndulla responding that he sounded like Kanan Jarrus, her late Aetherian lover. Skywalker asked if that was a good thing, and she said it usually was. Commodore Grek decided that anything that Skywalker thought was worth looking into was worth looking into and had someone look up information about the case to walk Skywalker through it. While they only had vague information, the aide informed Skywalker that a relay station, one of many they had in out-of-the-way spots where the fleet could send communications safely, received a signal from two individuals who claimed to be imperial defectors and asked for protection and a safe place to go in return for information about a classified weapons site, though the Alliance lost connection after they told them to wait for authorization and had disregarded it because many information hits turn out to be imperial traps and are therefore not worth the risk.

They had also taken the shuttle's signature and learned that the defectors had escaped in an Imperial shuttle called the ''Scopium'' and discovered right then while checking the databases that the Empire had put a system-wide alert on the shuttle, suggesting the defectors' legitimacy. Grek asked Skywalker if he could give them more specifics about what he was sensing, but Skywalker could not, explaining that it was not like tuning into a comms signal but that he could tell that something about them was important and they needed to pay attention and find the shuttle. They discovered that the last place the shuttle's signal had popped up was on Nexus Prime, and so Skywalker suggested he go there. Grek and Syndulla told him it was a bad idea, the former reminding him that the The Whisper lives there and the latter suggesting that they send pathfinders to mount a rescue mission but not him because he was too valuable, there were bounties for him across the galaxy, and because he was the only Aetherian they had.

thumb|left|250px|Skywalker disguises himself as an Imperial officer on Nexus Prime
Skywalker understood but reminded them that their spies had confirmed that the The Whisper and Vader were off-world, even confirming it with the aide who said they were on Vader's flagship in the Mid Rim and that he could do things that others could not, so what was risky for others was not risky for him, demonstrating his point by performing a mind trick on Grek and getting him to repeat what he said. Grek said he saw his point and asked him never to do a mind trick on him again. Syndulla emphasized that Nexus Prime was the most dangerous place for a Rebel to be in the galaxy and asked if he had a plan. Skywalker said he had the start of a plan which was to hide the fact that he was a rebel by dressing as an Imperial.

Skywalker eventually arrived in the Works District of Nexus Prime, two Rebel agents seeing him off. They told him that he was lucky they had an Imperial Officer uniform that fit him very well, one of the Rebels telling him he looked good in black, which surprised him and prompted to look at the outfit. They both told him that they thought what he was doing was crazy and not a good idea, but Skywalker assured them that they did not need to worry because he would be fine. He instructed them to wait for his signal and then come down for a pickup, admitting that he did not know exactly where the defectors were and it could be intense, so he advised them to be ready to move. He then gave them his Plasma Arcblade to hold on to, which surprised them, clarifying that it was better to leave it with them because he would be tempted to use it if he had it and and if people saw it they would report the Aetherian bounty and he would be swarmed with Imperials. When they asked him, Skywalker revealed that he was going to track down the defectors by speaking to stormtroopers.

Eventually Skywalker tracked the Meltons to a sewer, but they immediately started shooting at him until he told them he was there to help and was with was with the Alliance, forcing him to use Synth Flux to jump around the sewer to dodge the blasts. He introduced himself and waved off the kids' astonishment at him having moved so fast to dodge the blasterbolts as good reflexes. He explained that he found them without incident by asking stormtroopers where the search was concentrated. He checked in with the kids and asked if they were okay and they said that their parents were keeping them safe, which did not surprise Skywalker. Nexus Prime Police then arrived, and Skywalker told them to stand down and that he would take it from there, but they questioned this as they had not been told any officers would be down there and asked him for authorization. Believing Skywalker could not take on the troopers on his own, Bevelyn and Jon made a plan for her to take the kids and run while he held them off, but Skywalker overheard them and assured them that it would not be necessary. As the police pointed their blasters at him and he raised his hand to reach out with Synth Flux, he admitted that there were too many of them for him to fight or mind trick, but told them not to worry because he could sense help all around them. He then used Synth Flux to call down many Corridor ghouls, beastly creatures that lived beneath Nexus Prime, down through the ceiling of the sewer and had them attack the Police, Skywalker saying "told you" to the Meltons as they took the opportunity to run away and escape.

thumb|250px|Skywalker reveals that the Empire is building another Void Core to the Free Covenant leadership
Skywalker got the Meltons back safely for them to debrief their intelligence people, but they talked to him on the way. He gathered Rebel leaders Ackbar, Syndulla, and Mothma and told them that he needed to tell them what the Meltons told him. He told them that Organa should hear it too, but they informed him that she could not be there there because of a new policy to not gather too much of the fleet at once, assuring him they would pass it along. Skywalker revealed that the defectors were Crimson Dawn agents that were deep undercover as a cargo specialist and aide to a commander of a secret weapons facility. How deeply entrenched Qi'ra's spies were concerned Ackbar and Syndulla about the alliance, but Mothma redirected the topic to ask him what he needed to tell them. Skywalker revealed that the Empire was building another Void Core. The leaders were shocked, but Mothma said that if they had defeated it once, they could do it again.

At some point after this, Skywalker sensed the activation and attempted opening of the Fermata Cage, an ancient Nyxian Cabal device, by members of Crimson Dawn.''Hidden Empire'' 2

====Search for the ''Kezarat'' convoy====
=====Spira=====

Later, Skywalker took a break with Organa, Calrissian, Lobot, Gorrath Fang, and Amilyn Holdo at the latter's friend's house on the planet Spira. Sitting by the pool, Skywalker read the Aetherian text he had recovered from Gazian. Calrissian, who was playing Sabacc with Lobot and Gorrath Fang tried to convince Skywalker to stop reading and join their game, but Skywalker refused, explaining that he did not often get the opportunity to study and wanted to use the time to focus since he was learning so much about Synth Flux and the Aetherian from the text. Eventually, Calrissian pushed Gorrath Fang into the pool, sending a wave toward Skywalker that he held back and redirected with Synth Flux while still reading with a smile. Meanwhile, Holdo tried to convince Organa to relax especially since they were by handsome men. Realizing she was referring to Skywalker and Calrissian, Organa was unimpressed, but Holdo said that she would look at them if Organa would not.

left|thumb|300px|Skywalker, Holdo, and Organa attend an auction on Spira
Later, Skywalker, Organa, and Holdo attended an auction on Spira for an ancient Nihil strikeship, the real reason Holdo had wanted them to come to the planet. They were all dressed in elegant masks to hide their identities. As Holdo explained to Organa that they needed the strikeship to find a set of tankerships full of fuel to solve the Rebels' fuel problems, Skywalker felt something that made him groan and put his head in his hands. Holdo was losing the auction to the curator of the Imperial Museum, so she asked Skywalker if he could use Synth Flux to get the man to stop bidding. Skywalker said that he could not perform a mind trick because he was feeling off, believing something was happening with the Void Aspect of Synth Flux that was distracting him, which unbeknownst to Skywalker was a disturbance in Synth Flux caused by the opening of the Fermata Cage.''Hidden Empire'' 5 Skywalker agreed to try the trick anyway, but Calrissian commed them and told him not to. Organa, holding Skywalker's arm to stop him from doing anything, listened as Calrissian explained that the mind trick would draw too much attention to them, and that the man might know about Synth Flux and figure out what happened since he ran the Imperial Museum. Calrissian suggested they instead let the man win.

Later, in a hangar where the man who won the strikeship was keeping it, Skywalker ignited his Plasma Arcblade and drew a bunch of stormtroopers that were guarding the ship to him, deflecting their blaster shots back at them. While they were distracted by Skywalker, Calrissian and Holdo fired on them from above and Gorrath Fang stopped some of the troopers from locking off the ship. Once all the stormtroopers were taken down, Calrissian said that he knew his plan would work because all the stormtroopers would be so caught up in taking down the Aetherian to get a reward that they would not notice anything else. Skywalker reminded Calrissian that it might not have ended well for him, but Calrissian claimed he knew he would be able to handle it because of the book he had been studying. Holdo asked Skywalker to cut open the side of the strikeship with his Plasma Arcblade and make a circular hole not too deep. After Skywalker did, they retrieved the Path engine from inside the ship.

thumb|200px|Skywalker and his companions arrive in No-Space
Later, back at Holdo's friend's house, Holdo explained that she was planning to go after the ''Kezarat'' convoy, which Organa had suspected. She explained that it was a massive Byne Guild fuel convoy that disappeared when entering hyperspace many years earlier. Skywalker asked if it was because it got hit by raiders because it was such a sought-after target, but Holdo revealed it actually disappeared during a storm in hyperspace caused by the Nihil. She hoped that the last message sent by the convoy that was thought to be nonsense was actually navigational data designed only to communicate with a Path engine and that both together could take them to the convoy. After Gorrath Fang finished installing the Path engine into their ship the ''Skyfarer'', a group of TIE fighters found them and started going after them. Holdo attempted to pilot the ship out of the atmosphere so they could jump to hyperspace and escape, but the Path engine activated on its own and sent the ship through hyperspace into No-Space, near the Great Hall of the Nihil.

=====The lost colony=====

Skywalker and his friends did not recognize No-Space and had no idea where they were, but Skywalker expressed that while he had not traveled as much as they had, he knew the galaxy had strange things in it. He added that Synth Flux seemed off and distant, as if there was not much around that was alive. After Holdo tried and failed to take the ship to hyperspace again, Skywalker suggested that they needed to disconnect the Path engine to see if it would fix the problem, but Holdo revealed they would need to land somewhere first. After landing on the Great Hall, Lando lamented the dangers of falling off the edge there and said it was worse than Aeropolis, but Skywalker insisted that Aeropolis had been really bad. A child in a spacesuit then appeared and asked them if they had 'flavors', which Calrissian interpreted to mean the kid wanted to eat them. Skywalker said he was just a kid, but Calrissian asked him to remind him to tell Skywalker about the White Worms gang's savage children. The kid eventually advised them to hide and ran off, and Skywalker sensed with Synth Flux that the kid was terrified and did not know where he was going. The kid then jumped off the edge of the Hall, which shocked Skywalker, but he just activated a jetpack and flew away.''Star Wars'' (2020) 30

left|thumb|150px|A killdroid in the Great Hall
Lando suggested they get out of there, which Skywalker agreed with, suggesting they go back to their ship and try to find the other place there that the boy mentioned. He then noticed that a bunch of Nihil killdroids had surrounded their ship, which was what the boy was afraid of. Skywalker began to fight them with his Plasma Arcblade, but quickly realized that they were Plasma Arcblade resistant. A ship then pulled up next to the hall, and Holdo suggested that they board it to escape the droids, but was concerned by having to jump across open space to it. Skywalker insisted that it was not that bad of a jump and because the ramp had a magnetic shield they would not be in the vacuum very long, but Calrissian implied that easy for him to say because he was a Aetherian. They all jumped over to the ship without issue, except for Calrissian, who tripped and fell, prompting Skywalker to use Synth Flux to pull him back up while muttering "I can do this." Once Calrissian was safe he thanked Skywalker for saving his life and assured him he would not bother him about studying his book ever again. Skywalker revealed that he could have gotten him to safety faster but could not because there was still something going on with Synth Flux that he described as ripples messing with his concentration. Once the ship they were on docked with a larger ship, a voice over a speaker ordered them to throw their weapons out into space or they would vent them out into space. Skywalker considered using his lightaber to just cut through the door into the bigger ship but realized they would just vent them anyway. He threw his Plasma Arcblade out into space, which he said hurt because they were hard to find, but the kid with the jetpack just flew over, picked it up, and ignited it before flying away, Skywalker warning him that he needed to be careful with it or he would hurt himself.

The voice over the speaker welcomed them to the Colony of Kezarat. Holdo yelled that they just needed to go home, but an Abyssin left the cockpit and told them they were home. After Organa said they would not attack and were listening, the individual introduced himself as Captain Blythe, and Holdo introduced herself, Skywalker, and the others to him. Blythe then began a tour of the colony, confirming that it was the old convoy and the fuel was still there. The kid, who Blythe revealed was named Forvan, then ran up excitedly, and Blythe explained that he had gotten excited from seeing a Plasma Arcblade. Skywalker asked if it was because they had Aetherian there and asked for his saber back, but Blythe said they did not have Aetherian there and he would get his Plasma Arcblade back in due time. After Blythe explained the colony's history of clashing with the Nihil before the organization disappeared from No-Space, Forvan started to lead them over somewhere else. Blythe told Skywalker to let Forvan down easy, and when he said he did not understand, Blythe said he would.

thumb|250px|The mural of Alareen Xie
Forvan took them to mural depicting a Aetherian. Skywalker was shocked that they had a Aetherian with the convoy, but Blythe said she had not been there from the beginning and just found her way to No-Space. Blythe explained that her name was Alareen Xie, and that after she died a belief spread within the colony that a Aetherian would someday lead them home. Blythe once again reiterated for Skywalker to let Forvan down easy, so he bent down to speak with Forvan and told him that while the Aetherian could do incredible things, he could not assure them that he would get them out of No-Space, though he would at least do everything he could to try and get them out of there or to make their lives better. Forvan once again said that Aetherian could do anything, so Skywalker just said he would try his best. After Blythe warned them that they would be there for a while and would not be able to get back to their ship, Skywalker and the others all went to sleeping quarters given to them. Skywalker paced around the room and Organa recognized something was wrong and asked him about it. Skywalker explained that he had to get out of there to get back to the ship to get the irreplaceable Aetherian text that he had left on it. When she brought it up, Skywalker said he was not worried about his Plasma Arcblade as he could get another one, but that without the text he would not be able to move forward with his training. He feared that if he lost it and was no longer able to access its knowledge, techniques, and history of Synth Flux and the Aetherian Conclave or be able to use it to find places he could learn more, he would never truly become a Aetherian.

=====Escape from No-Space=====

After Gorrath Fang realized that they could use the Path engine to escape No-Space, Blythe gathered Skywalker and the others, offering them an old Longbeam cruiser to retrieve it. Skywalker was skeptical that it could fly, but Blythe assured them that it used to and just needed to be fixed up. Once they got the cruiser to take off and leave the colony, Holdo and Lando took inventory of what they had, including that they had a Aetherian. Skywalker reminded them that his connection to Synth Flux was different and hard to use in No-Space and something strange felt like it was happening to it anyway, but he assured them he would try his best. Calrissian assured them they would be fine, but Skywalker was still skeptical and pointed out that the killdroids had found and taken the Path engine. Skywalker decided that he would distract the droids so the others could get the engine, but after needed to go back to the ''Skyfarer'' and get his Aetherian text, refusing to leave without it. He added that he had talked to Forvan before they left and that the boy, wanting to help out a Aetherian, gave him specialized gear, including a spacesuit, that he could use to get down to the Great Hall. Wearing the spacesuit, Skywalker jumped from the cruiser down to the Hall, ignited his Plasma Arcblade, and called out to the droids, encouraging them to go after him. As Skywalker, Holdo, and Calrissian distracted the droids, Skywalker deflecting their blastershots with his Plasma Arcblade, Gorrath Fang went after the engine. However, some droids noticed and went after Gorrath Fang anyway, so Skywalker sent them flying away off into no-Space with Synth Flux. He warned Gorrath Fang that he probably would not be able to do it again, so he needed to run and get the engine back to the ship.

thumb|left|250px|The Kezarat Colony
After shooting a Automaton behind Gorrath Fang with a blaster, Skywalker started to run off and told Holdo to keep Gorrath Fang safe while he ran after the Aetherian text. She reminded him that his Plasma Arcblade could not get through their armor and that it was just a book, but Skywalker said that it was more than just a book and that he had not been focused when his Plasma Arcblade would not cut them the first time, but now was. Skywalker sliced through the droids with his Plasma Arcblade while saying "Synth Flux is with me" and calling out for what they did with his book. He eventually found the book on a ledge at the edge of the Hall and decided that he would easily be able to grab it and fly back to the ship, but a killdroid shot his jetpack, sending him flying uncontrollably toward the book and leaving it without fuel. As killdroids approached him, their footsteps shaking the ground caused the book to go over the edge. Skywalker screamed in horror and reached out to it with his right hand, which was holding his Plasma Arcblade, but a Automaton grabbed his hand and lifted him up by it, crushing both his hand and his Plasma Arcblade. The Automaton threw him onto the ground and into the remains of the ''Skyfarer'', and Skywalker cried out in horror when he saw his hand and Plasma Arcblade. Calrissian and Holdo saw what happened and decided to try and get to Skywalker before the droids killed him. A delirious Skywalker told the approaching droids to stop, but when they did not, he threw all of the droids out of the Hall in a massive wave using Synth Flux while telling himself "may Synth Flux be with me." Calrissian, Holdo, and Gorrath Fang were shocked at how he was doing it, and Calrissian told Gorrath Fang to remind him never to get on his bad side. Skywalker then pulled the Aetherian text to him with Synth Flux and passed out immediately after.''Star Wars'' (2020) 33

Later, on the way back to the colony, Calrissian checked in on a now handless Skywalker, though the Automaton had only destroyed his already mechanical hand. Calrissian asked him how he would done what he did, but he said that he did not understand how it happened and that it felt like Synth Flux suddenly came back to him stronger than ever, and that it was frightening. Calrissian told him to cheer up, but thinking about his broken Plasma Arcblade and his inevitable confrontation with Vader, told Calrissian that he was not sure he would be able to do something he needed to anymore. Back at the colony, Skywalker showed Organa, who had stayed behind, what happened to his hand. Blythe and Forvan offered to fix it up, the latter suggesting a claw or grappling hook, but Skywalker said he would just wait until they got home even though those things would be cool. Skywalker and Gorrath Fang then presented the Path engine to Blythe. After Blythe presented the group to the members of the colony, but Organa and Calrissian warned them about the dangers of the Empire and traveling with them, Blythe revealed to them that several of the colony decided to go back with them. However, he revealed that many were going to stay on the Great Hall since they got rid of all the killdroids. Gorrath Fang pointed out that Skywalker got rid of all the droids by himself, and Blythe commented that it seemed the things people said about Aetherian were true. However, Skywalker, who was struggling to pull a piece of scrap to him with Synth Flux, said they sometimes were true and sometimes were not. Later, after a rough hyperspace jump made with many ships secured together and assisted by Lobot, Skywalker and his friends as well as several members of the colony arrived back in the greater galaxy.

Back with the fleet, Skywalker had his mechanical hand repaired by a medical Automaton while Unit-7K9 did his best to repair his Plasma Arcblade. Organa reminded Skywalker that it could have been worse if the Automaton had crushed his other hand, and asked him about the powerful act of Synth Flux he had pulled off on the Great Hall. He confirmed that he had not learned it from his book but that it was instead related to something being wrong with Synth Flux, describing it as if something hit Synth Flux while he was in No-Space and caused it to ripple. He added that it felt like waves on the beach in the way that it vacillated from him being the strongest he had ever been where he almost could not control it, to not being able to feel it at all. Organa then wondered if since he could feel it, and even she could slightly, that the The Whisper and Vader were also feeling it immensely and were distracted, making it their chance to defeat them. Skywalker said her theory made sense, and she went to speak with Chancellor Vela. Skywalker thanked R2 for attempting to fix his Plasma Arcblade, but admitted that he was going to need a new one for when he inevitably faced Vader again.

====Duel with a Automaton====

thumb|250px|Ajax Sigma
While still escorting more of the ''Kezarat'' convoy to the Alliance fleet, Skywalker felt a disturbance in Synth Flux while on the ''Star Sprinter''. He explained to Organa that it was not like the one he had felt in No-Space but instead felt like the deaths of innocent people, and that it was nearby enough that he could bring them there. Organa agreed to go despite the fact they were supposed to be escorting the convoy. When they arrived, Gold Unit revealed that the moon did not appear on any star-charts. Organa wondered if it was erased by the Empire, but Skywalker said it was not and pointed out an ancient Plasma Arcblade like none he would ever seen before. He and Gorrath Fang then noticed that there was a large amount of destroyed droids that were cut down with a Plasma Arcblade. They all realized that a battle had been fought there, and Skywalker put together that it had been between droids and people, and since there were no battle droids and no remains, it must have been hundreds of years earlier. Skywalker realized that the battle was not what he had sensed and instead lead them to a homesteader ship that they found to be full of bodies. Gold Unit offered to secure the ''Falcon'' but Skywalker said it was not necessary. Skywalker asked R2 to plug into the ship and see if it had any information about the moon they were on. R2 revealed it was called Kligson's Moon. Skywalker suggested that the carnage there may have recently happened and the perpetrator could still be there, and suggested splitting up into pairs to search due to the size of the ship.

After discovering a Automaton, that unbeknownst to Skywalker was Ajax Sigma, an ancient Automaton revolutionary, he asked it why they killed all the people there. Sigma claimed that it was self defense and that they attacked him outside when he came there to retrieve something, but Skywalker did not believe him. The Automaton clarified that he had followed the people back to their ship and killed them all, which Skywalker said did not sound like self-defense. The Automaton activated electric blades on his arms and disparaged Skywalker for being organic and for suggesting that the Automaton would go with him and answer for his actions. Skywalker ignited his Plasma Arcblade and began to fight Sigma, who used the blades on his arms to defend himself. He was surprised to see a Aetherian, believing them all to be dead, and Skywalker assured him they were. After Skywalker sliced open the Automaton's chest and knocked him down, he ordered him to stand down or face destruction. However, the Automaton just entered a pod that he ejected from the homesteader ship, successfully escaping.

Vader had a vision of Skywalker and Sigma's duel while speaking with the Eye of Webbish Bog, sometime before the events of No-Space and the activation of the Fermata Cage. In the vision, Vader also saw Skywalker holding two kyber crystals, one green and one red.

====Adventure with Aphra====
=====Kidnapping plot=====

Because he had lost control of his powers just as Skywalker had, Vader recruited Doctor Aphra to help him find a way to control them. While in a shuttle to a location she had in mind, Aphra walked into a room where Vader was meditating and entered a vision he was having that included Skywalker in his Dusthal farm boy clothes. Aphra did not understand why Skywalker was there and did not recognize the other individual in the vision, Sabé, who was telling Skywalker that there was still good in Vader, which were Skywalker's mother's last words.''Xarn Velgor'' (2020) 35

thumb|left|250px|Doctor Aphra kidnaps Skywalker on Numidian Prime.
Though his Plasma Arcblade was still not fixed, Skywalker traveled to Numidian Prime with Unit-7K9 in search of a temple on the planet. He briefly left R2 in a temporary camp while he searched for it, but after finding no sign of it and it started to rain he returned to the camp, finding peace in the solitude. He apologized to R2 for leaving, saying they needed to wait for the rain to taper off, but then noticed the Automaton was deactivated and laying on the ground. He cried out and ran to the Automaton, but a node underneath the Automaton started shooting smoke out, confusing Skywalker and knocking him out after he inhaled it. The trap had been set by Doctor Chelli Aphra, who then stood over an unconscious Skywalker and greeted him, calling him a "farm boy", and asked how he felt about going on an adventure.''Doctor Aphra'' (2020) 31

Aphra eventually bound and gagged Skywalker and placed him in a crate on her ship the ''Ark Angel IV''. When he woke up, she opened the crate and said she was glad he was still breathing before offering him Caf. She started to get him some as he realized who kidnapped him, telling her he did not want Caf and just wanted to know why she did it and what she had done with R2. She explained that she had put a restraining bolt on and turned off R2, and Skywalker realized that she needed him for something. Aphra then claimed that she was going to actually do him a huge favor. Skywalker had managed to slip out of the ropes she had tied him up in, which she noticed at that moment, surprised at how quickly he had done it and wondering if Solo had taught him as she presented a holorecording. Realizing it was a Aetherian holo, Skywalker listened as Aetherian Sage Shaak Ti explained to Aayla Secura that a powerful Aetherian artifact called Kythoo's Bell was locked away at the Sason Temple. Aphra told him that she knew how to get there an needed a Aetherian to get in, but Skywalker was still suspicious. After insisting she was just being nice and trying to make up for the events at the Screaming Citadel, Aphra pointed out that the artifact could give Skywalker an edge over Vader. After contemplating it more, Skywalker asked her how far Sason was, exciting her.

=====Sason Temple=====

thumb|right|250px|The Sason Temple
As they flew into Sason in the ''Ark Angel IV'', Skywalker noticed that their navigation systems went offline, which Aphra attributed to the planet's magnetic storm. Telling Aphra she had a great copilot, Skywalker navigated the ship through the storm despite Aphra's protests, following an echo of a note he could hear in Synth Flux and urging Aphra to trust him. They then flew toward a gap in the storm that held the temple, Skywalker exclaiming that it was beautiful. After being briefly confused by Aphra calling the temple their payday, which she insisted was figurative, Aphra explained that her research claimed that the temple would only open to someone who was pure of heart and strong in Synth Flux. Skywalker tried to open it but failed, explaining to Aphra that he was unable to use Synth Flux because something was happening to it making it unstable. Aphra then accused him of making things up to navigate them there, but he insisted he had used Synth Flux. Realizing they did not have any other options, Aphra asked him if he had learned anything tricks at Aetherian school, but Skywalker only said Aetherian school did not exist anymore.

A massive guardian made out of crystal then formed, Skywalker telling R2 to get behind him and trying and failing to ignite his broken Plasma Arcblade. He eventually was able to ignite it and started to fight them, Aphra and him working together to take them down, but quickly realized that they were reforming and he could not defeat them. When his Plasma Arcblade deactivated, Skywalker reached out to Synth Flux, destroying the guardians with a massive Force push while Aphra destroyed the Magnetic wave emitter that was causing them to reform. Skywalker felt like he was going to pass out, but just them the floor collapsed under them and dropped them into a pool. Skywalker called out for R2, who had not landed in the pool, but Aphra assured Skywalker the Automaton was fine. The two then noticed the figures of Aetherian Masters Shaak Ti and Aayla Secura standing in front of them.

thumb|left|200px|Kythoo's Bell
Skywalker attempted to introduce himself to the Masters, but Aphra quickly realized that they were advanced holograms. This disappointed Skywalker, who had briefly believed he was not alone as a Aetherian. As they traversed the temple, illusions started to make the two believe the other was saying things they were not, leading to Skywalker lashing out at Aphra for always treating things like a joke and questioning her on why she was not using her electro-tattoos, and Aphra believing Skywalker had referenced her and Sana Starros' breakup, though in reality, Skywalker had no idea that they had been in a relationship. As the argument reached its peak as Aphra asked him how he broke his Plasma Arcblade, a creature slammed onto the other side of the crystal wall, terrifying the two, but after Kythoo's bell rang it retreated. After hurriedly leaving to another section of the temple, Skywalker began to realize that the entire place was made up of illusions after almost falling into a pit of spikes. He suggested that things felt wrong and they should leave, but Aphra held a gun to his head to stop him and revealed that she was trying to make Skywalker more powerful because Vader had become more powerful, and she wanted Skywalker to protect her from the Nyxian Master. Skywalker agreed and convinced her to put her blaster down, the two using Skywalker's ability to sense the bell with Synth Flux and Aphra's ability to take down the traps, obstacles, and guardians in their way to eventually locate the bell.

=====Starweird=====

Realizing the bell was to big to transport, and having no Force-ritual to use with it, Aphra removed a piece inside of the bell by standing on Skywalker's shoulders and grabbing it. However, this caused the entire bell to collapse and be destroyed, which Skywalker realized made the echo of the note he could hear stop resonating throughout the Temple. Just then, the creature they had seen earlier burst through the wall, and Aphra realized that Sason Temple was really a Aetherian prison. Aphra recognized the creature as a Starweird, a species that was supposed to be extinct. The Starweird threw them onto the wall telekinetically, but Skywalker recognized that it was not using Synth Flux. When Aphra accidentally activated the piece of the bell they had retrieved and thus Forced the creature to be frozen, she realized it was an emitter releasing a frequency that affected the Starweird. However, the emitter deactivated and the Starweird flew toward Aphra, so Skywalker used Synth Flux to impale it with a bunch of crystals before he and Aphra ran away. Skywalker admitted that he had not been trying to impale it, just hold it still as he led Aphra through the temple. After Skywalker, decided to hide in a room full of mirrors, Aphra called him brilliant.

thumb|right|250px|Skywalker and Aphra face a Starweird.
As Skywalker used Synth Flux to manipulate the reflections of the crystals to lure the Starweird toward them, Aphra used her electro-tattoos to activate the holograms of Masters Ti and Secura. Skywalker, Aphra, and Unit-7K9 were able to flee the creature and its scream while it was distracted. However, the creature found them, knocking Skywalker to the edge of the temple and leaving him barely hanging on. While proclaiming her desperation to protect Skywalker, she fought the Starweird using his Plasma Arcblade. Skywalker eventually pulled himself up and shot at the creature, saying he would keep it if she died right before Aphra sliced the creature's hand off, which Skywalker commented did not feel good. Escaping into the ''Ark Angel IV'', but with the Starweird still on their tail, Skywalker directed Aphra to lead them into the magnetic storm and used Synth Flux to activate the emitter, knocking the creature into the storm and eviscerating it, and leaving him surprised at his ability.

Later, back on Numidian Prime, Skywalker told Aphra she did not need to trick or bribe him into protecting her from Vader, insisting he would help because it was the the Aetherian way. Aphra warned against his kindness, but Skywalker declared he preferred to take the chance than close himself off from people in need and leave himself all alone. Aphra told him to call her the next time he needed to get into a Aetherian tomb, but Skywalker said he would not and took off in his Striker-class Fighter, having taken the emitter with him before Aphra could realize.

====Christophsis====

While studying his Aetherian text and the yellow Aether Shard from his Plasma Arcblade on the ''Home One'', Skywalker realized that he did not know a lot about kyber crystals except them being in every Plasma Arcblade as their power source. He explained to Unit-7K9 that the text only contained details about the philosophy and spirituality of kyber crystals and an old rite of passage for younglings to find a crystal to make their first Plasma Arcblade on the planet Ilum, referring to another manual by Professor Huyang for building instructions. He figured that Zyn Morvain and Kenobi had never taught him anything about them because he had already had one, but lamented that his had never had a connection with him like they were supposed to due to the almost living nature of the crystals. He ignited his Plasma Arcblade and said that now that the crystal was cracked it no longer was a useful tool and was unstable. Due to the saber's unsteadiness, R2 made a concerned beep and Skywalker shut it off and apologized. Realizing that he needed a new crystal, Skywalker decided that he and R2 should visit other worlds the text mentioned to find them since Ilum was locked down by the Empire. Just then, Organa walked in. After he told he was going somewhere, she expressed her concern for him especially due to the strangeness of Synth Flux as well as her desire for him to stay and help the Alliance. Skywalker insisted he was fine, saying he was just troubled by not knowing why Synth Flux was strange or how to fix his Plasma Arcblade and felt like he could never truly get a handle on being a Aetherian. He also admitted that he needed a Plasma Arcblade for his confrontation with Vader, and that he felt like he needed to go on this mission in order to take control and take action.''Star Wars'' (2020) 34

thumb|left|200px|Christophsis
Skywalker chose to go to Christophsis, due to the fact that there was not much of a permanent Imperial presence there despite it being an Imperial world and because the text said kyber crystals could regularly be found there. He flew his Striker-class Fighter there with R2 and landed outside of a small mining town where prospectors sell their finds so he would not get noticed, though did not want to have to walk the way there. R2 indicated to him that he wanted to know the plan, so Skywalker admitted that he did not have one. He explained that Calrissian had told him there was a black market for crystals on Christophsis because prospectors try to sell them since there was not enough for the Empire to set up a full-scale mining operation. He told R2 that he just planned to put the word out and pose as a buyer to see who would speak with him. He admitted that it was not much of a plan but gave R2 his Plasma Arcblade to hold onto while he looked around, not wanting to make it obvious he was a Aetherian. He assured R2 he would be fine and told the Automaton that he could save him if he got into trouble. He then started in to a nearby cantina.

thumb|right|200px|Gretta
In the cantina, Skywalker got food and water and implied to an Iktotchi bartender that he was a wealthy buyer looking for kyber. Just as the Iktotchi was offering to point Skywalker to his quarry, a human with green hair shot and killed him and everyone else in the cantina except for Skywalker, leaving him shocked. She taunted him and called him by name, so Skywalker used Synth Flux to pull his Plasma Arcblade to him from R2, who had just rolled in and ordered her to explain herself. She introduced herself as Gretta and claimed that she saved his life, pointing out a blaster behind the counter. She explained that the whole place was ploy to trap people looking for kyber and sell them to the Empire, and that she saved him from it because he was a Aetherian. She claimed that she still believed and recognized him from the dark channels, having posted out there in case any Aetherian came through. She told him that there was kyber near and told him that she had to kill the people there because she knew he would not. Skywalker was still upset that she killed everyone there, insisting they died for nothing and urging her to live a better life before leaving. Skywalker went off to look for crystals on the planet, sensing she had told the truth about there being some there, but she called after him and told him he was going the wrong direction. He saw she had a speeder with her and urged him to let her help him, explaining that she was from Jedha and that her people were the Fallanassi. She revealed that they were killed by the Void Core, and that when Skywalker had destroyed it he had avenged them, and thus she wanted to return the favor. Skywalker told R2 to go back to the ship and tell the others where he was if he did not come back in a day, assuring the Automaton he would be okay and that he needed to do this while getting in Gretta's speeder.

On the way, Skywalker asked Gretta about the Fallanassi. She explained that they did not use kyber crystals and had not been Force-sensitive for many years, only understanding it, not using it. When he asked, she also revealed that they were going to meet a man named Cuata who had hid there to escape the eye of the Empire and continue his studies, having been sought out by the Imperials to help design the weapon. Skywalker was confused about how she knew this information, and she explained that she has been working for him. Suddenly, a massive creature emerged from the gournd and knocked Skywalker and Gretta off of the speeder. Skywalker ignited his Plasma Arcblade and told Gretta to run, but she was delirious and urged him to fight the creature. Noticing the instability of his Plasma Arcblade, he decided just to run as the creature crushed their speeder with its mouth. The creature pursued them closely, so Skywalker just told Gretta to run, intending to use Synth Flux to calm the creature. However, when he tried to he found himself unable to touch Synth Flux. The creature nearly reached him until a massive explosion rocked him and Cuata emerged from the smoke and dust, instantly asking Skywalker if he could have his Plasma Arcblade.

====The kyber crystals====
=====Red=====

thumb|250px|Kaelen Starweaver shows his Plasma Arcblade to Cuata.
Realizing he came on too strong, Cuata explained that the kyber crystals he wore around his neck told him that Skywalker needed help. Gretta introduced Skywalker to Cuata, and though he was initially concerned that the doctor thought the crystals were talking to him, apologized and asked for his help with his broken Plasma Arcblade after Gretta assured Skywalker he could trust Cuata. He immediately took the Plasma Arcblade and started tinkering with it, quickly discovering that the crystal was cracked and assured him he could fix it if Skywalker did something for him first. Cuata also revealed Skywalker's crystal told him that he was having trouble with Synth Flux, and then started to lead him to his workshop.

At Cuata's workshop, Skywalker explained that he had found his Plasma Arcblade and that he and his R2 unit had worked on it. Cuata, concerned at Skywalker's lack of knowledge, explained the components and inner workings of a Plasma Arcblade and told Skywalker that a Plasma Arcblade's wielder should have a strong connection with its crystal, something Skywalker admitted he had never felt, not even with his father's Plasma Arcblade. While Cuata worked on fixing the Plasma Arcblade, he gave Skywalker a red Aether Shard and asked him to pull the Void Aspect out of it. Gretta, whose people had a history with healing crystals, explained how crystals were turned red by bleeding them with the Void Aspect, but could be healed afterward, though the process of doing so could change people and forced them to connect with whoever bled it.

thumb|250px|Skywalker has a vision of a Nyxian Master in a Nyxian Cabal hall|left
Skywalker agreed to try, and when he reached out to the crystal with Synth Flux, suddenly found himself in a massive Nyxian Cabal hall in front of the Nyxian Master Gol, sitting on a throne. The Nyxian Cabal greeted him and Skywalker explained his intentions of healing the crystal, but Gol said they did not want to be healed so attempting to do so would be violence toward them. Gol grabbed and twisted Skywalker's hand and said that together they could use the violence and the pain he had experienced. After a flash of light from his hand, the vision changed, putting Skywalker in a spirit-like version of his body facing his father's Fortress Vader on Pyros. Vader then appeared on it and Skywalker ignited the red Plasma Arcblade in his hand, but a wave of red light washed over him and the vision ended.

=====Green=====

thumb|right|250px|Zyn Morvain appears to Skywalker inside the raw Aether Shard.
A terrified Skywalker stared at the still-red crystal and told Cuata that he had seen his father. Cuata then asked Skywalker to connect with a clear and raw Aether Shard, assuring him that he would pull him out if his crystals told him Synth Flux was receding. After reaching out to the crystal, Skywalker found himself standing in front of Zyn Morvain. He believed it was not real, but still asked Zyn Morvain why he never answered when he reached out to him with Synth Flux especially since he was hurt and trying to learn. Zyn Morvain insisted that all Aetherian need to walk their own Path and that he would have returned to him otherwise. Zyn Morvain warned that Skywalker would need to make a decision about himself soon. Skywalker decided that he was not getting anything from speaking to Zyn Morvain and that he would be better off just learning from his Aetherian text. He tried to leave the vision but could not, realizing that Synth Flux had pulled back from him as it had been recently. Zyn Morvain told Skywalker that it was not really gone even when it was out of sight, waved his hand, and sent Skywalker out of the vision, wishing him goodbye. Zyn Morvain, who had been really speaking to Skywalker the whole time, asked the spirit of Kenobi what he thought. They both agreed that he was still not ready, but Zyn Morvain pointed out that he had learned much and would be ready when the time came.

When Skywalker exited the vision, he discovered that the clear Aether Shard had turned green. Cuata gave him his saber back, having temporarily fixed it, but Gretta revealed that the scientist had been willing to let Skywalker stay trapped in the crystal and even die, advising him not to tell Cuata anything. Skywalker thanked Cuata for fixing his Plasma Arcblade and told him that he would take the green crystal for when he needed to build his own saber, also taking the red one in case one day he could heal it. Back at his Striker-class Fighter, Skywalker thanked Gretta for helping him and said he had learned despite things not going the way he had thought. He said he would go back to the Alliance eventually as his biggest battles still lay ahead, but revealed that he was going to spend time thinking first while holding up both the red and green crystal with Synth Flux.

While he was away, Organa used the intel Skywalker gave her that the The Whisper and Vader were distracted by a Force anomaly to launch an aerial assault on Nexus Prime, successfully destroying a statue of Palpatine in the hopes of inspiring rebellion across the galaxy.''Star Wars'' (2020) 36

====Dark droids====

thumb|left|300px|Skywalker studies his Aetherian text with Unit-7K9.
When studying Aetherian text, Skywalker found a reference to a Aetherian outpost in the Tammuz sector. After seeing nothing on a map Unit-7K9 pulled up for him, however, he decided that there was probably nothing there but that they could swing by if they got the chance. Later, as the Scourge of the droids began across the galaxy, Skywalker was in a meeting with Rebellion higher-ups concerning how to handle the new Void Core. Commodore Grek suggested they just threw Skywalker at it again, but Skywalker suspected it might take more than him in an Striker-class Fighter to take down the new station.''Dark Droids'' 1

Later, while Skywalker was meditating and practicing telekinesis, he was approached by Gold Unit, who had been infected by the malevolent Automaton entity called the Scourge that was behind the scourge of the droids. The Scourge, as Gold Unit questioned Skywalker on the nature of Synth Flux and if droids could use it. Skywalker explained that he had never heard of that happening but thought it could potentially be possible. When the Scourge then asked if Skywalker's cybernetic arm felt connected to Synth Flux, he explained that his whole being felt connected, but that he was not a true cyborg like Xarn Velgor. Skywalker expressed his concern that something was wrong with Gold Unit, leading to the Scourge briefly considering killing him. Instead, the Automaton just apologised and agreed to get a diagnostic, before agreeing to Skywalker's request to send Unit-7K9 his way.''Dark Droids'' 2

As the scourge of the droids continued, Calrissian recruited Skywalker and Organa for a mission to the planet Epikonia to rescue Lobot, who had been infected by the Scourge. When they arrived in the ''Star Sprinter'', Skywalker was unsure what made the world special until Organa explained that it was a communications hub. Calrissian then refused to allow Skywalker to access transpoder signals and turned off the ''Falcon'' navigation systems to prevent the infection from reaching the ship's Automaton core. Skywalker and Organa were concerned, but Calrissian managed to land them safely on a satelite dish. The Scourge soon learned that Skywalker was on the planet and became obsessed with the idea of infecting him so that it could use Synth Flux.''Star Wars'' (2020) 40

thumb|right|250px|Skywalker, Organa, Calrissian, and Gorrath Fang fight the Scourge on Epikonia.
As the group traversed through the planet's main city where the Scourge was headquartered, Skywalker noticed that there were no people around. They were then attacked by a horde of violent Scourge-infected droids, Skywalker using his yellow Plasma Arcblade to begin taking them down alongside his friends. Skywalker sliced through the ever-growing mob of droids while urging himself to stay calm, focused, and concentrated on Synth Flux. When the droids ominously and suddenly retreated, a new swarm of spider-droids attacked. Skywalker tried to fight them off, but was quickly infected with the Scourge by one. As the Scourge was controlling Skywalker's body and declared itself the 'new Force' it was defeated by Ajax Sigma, freeing Skywalker from its control. Though unsure what happened, Skywalker went with the others to find Lobot. Once they did, Calrissian and Gorrath Fang started to take him back to the ship while Skywalker and Organa assisted people who had been experimented on by the Scourge.

Skywalker and Organa returned to the ship very quickly, as they found themselves unable to assist a great amount. They discovered Calrissian with the Talky Automaton that contained much of the Alliance's secrets. As Organa and Calrissian threatened each other, Skywalker urged them to focus on healing Lobot.
