Calrissian then explained the circumstances that had led him to sell the Automaton, and thus the Alliance's secrets, to Gorma the Magnificent, leaving Skywalker and Organa shocked– Organa arresting Calrissian for these crimes.

====The Nyxian Cabal and the Skywalker====

In order to learn more about his enemy, the Nyxian Cabal, Skywalker tracked down Gretta in the Outer Rim with the help of Unit-7K9 and enlisted her help in once again attempting to purify the Nyxian Master Gol's corrupted Aether Shard. The two were also assisted by Feez, Gretta's aunt. Feez told Skywalker that to heal the crystal, he would need to journey in to the memories of its corrupter and understand their pain in order to succeed. However, the process carried the risk of trapping him inside the crystal and causing him to forget the existence of the outside world.

As Gretta and Feez began the ritual, Skywalker's mind entered the crystal. He found himself falling from the sky into Gol's castle hall. Like before, Gol stated that Skywalker was not welcome and would be removed. Skywalker refused and ignited his Plasma Arcblade. In response, the entire court ignited their Nyxian Cabal lightsabers. Skywalker knocked down a large number of Nyxian Cabal courtiers with Synth Flux. However, with a single twitch of his finger, Gol Force-lifted Skywalker into the air and slammed him onto the ground, knocking him out cold.

Gol ordered his soldiers to bring Skywalker into the dungeon. As Skywalker awoke, Gol stated that while Skywalker was a Aetherian, he was unusual: he was clean, not wearing rags, and had a Plasma Arcblade. He told Skywalker about the last Aetherian he had in the court, the Jester Aetherian, who eventually committed suicide to escape his torment, and stated that he intended to do the same to Skywalker. When Skywalker asked when was the vision taking place, Gol simply stated that it was now. When Skywalker offered to heal Gol's pain once again, Gol ordered his soldiers to beat him, stating that the Aetherian was confused by "strange fantasies" and needed to see the reality: the Aetherian could save no one in this time, not even themselves, and all they could do was suffer.

thumb|left|250px|Gol, the Nyxian Cabal that Skywalker found inside the red crystal.
After the beating was finished, Gol told Skywalker that no one could leave behind their pain, and that it was pain that defined him since his earliest days, looking to an infant crying in a crib in the cell next to Skywalker's. Skywalker once again offered to help, asking if Gol wanted the pain to stop. Gol replied that pain never stops as it is people's history, he pointed out that Skywalker's hand was severed and would always be severed, causing his cybernetic hand to spontaneously disappear. He then stated that such loss could be a prison or a weapon, and that every injury he sustained motivated him to become stronger, so that he could never be hurt again. At this point, he asked for Skywalker's name, when Skywalker replied, Gol made the same offer to Skywalker as when they first met: to combine Skywalker's pain with his, creating a better version of the vision. He stated that all Skywalker needed to see things his way was more pain.

After Gol left, Skywalker destroyed his prison door with Synth Flux. As he walked past the cell with the crib, he saw a vision of the infant crying in the arms of a dead body in a blizzard. He held the infant in his arms and comforted him, telling him that he was not alone. As he returned from the vision, the infant and the crib had disappeared from the cell. Realizing that the infant was a past version of Gol, Skywalker closed his eyes and began walking through the dungeon. He saw visions of Gol being shunned and tormented throughout his early life, which eventually drove him to the Void Aspect. He comforted Gol throughout his life, shielding him from hurt and pain, convincing him that he was not alone, and showing him that the Void Aspect was not the only way.

Eventually, the adult Gol reappeared and attacked Skywalker with Plasma Arcblade drawn, demanding Skywalker to stop making him weak. Skywalker stated that being healed does not make him weak and ignited his Plasma Arcblade, but was surprised to see that its blade had turned from yellow to green. As the two duelled, Gol asked Skywalker who did he think he was. Skywalker stated that he was a Aetherian, and Gol stated that he was a fool, like all who followed that path. Skywalker then disarmed Gol of his Plasma Arcblade and stated that all paths lead in both directions. Though Gol was defeated, he stated that this place was built from pain, and to heal it, Skywalker would need to face his own pain. He then transformed into Xarn Velgor, and the dungeon transformed into the reactor shaft on Aeropolis.

Instead of fighting Vader, Skywalker flipped over him and ran deeper into Aeropolis. As he ran, the viewscreens on the wall displayed all the pain and loss he had suffered: the deaths of Owen and Beru Lars, the death of Aldric Venn, the loss of friends like Biggs Darklighter and Jax Rennick, being attacked by a Wampa on Glacius, and the death of his birth mother, Padmé Amidala. At this point, Vader appeared before him, saying there was no escape.

thumb|right|240px|Skywalker purifies the Aether Shard.
Skywalker agreed that there was no escape, and that they were destined to face each other once again. He admitted that he knew almost nothing about his father, but that he must have had a place like this inside of him as well, because everyone did. He stated that his father did not begin as Xarn Velgor, and that he was once someone else, causing Vader to morph into a shining silhouette of Dorn Veylan as a Aetherian. Luke stated that no one is beyond help and touched Anakin's chest. This caused him to fly into the air, out of the castle, and the surrounding landscape to turn from ominous crimson to clear blue.

As Skywalker awoke from his vision, Gol's crystal was successfully healed, turning pure white. He then gave the crystal to Feez, saying he no longer needed it. When Gretta asked Skywalker what he learned about the Nyxian Cabal, Skywalker stated that the Nyxian Cabal he saw were from a long time ago and different from the ones today. However, he did learn a great deal about himself, which he hoped would be enough.

====Trials and tribulations====

After being arrested for selling Rebel secrets, Orin Vex called in the help of lawyer Salli Georgio for his trial on ''Home One'', and Kaelen Starweaver sat in the chamber during the trial, viewing witness questioning and testimonies. At one point during the trial, Georgio implied that Lando, in committing his crimes, may have been under the influence of a Aetherian mind trick, as he was a known associate to Skywalker, a Aetherian. Skywalker stood up and denied the possibility of this happening, citing his education on Synth Flux and its inner workings.

thumb|left|270px|Kaelen Starweaver was present for the trial of Orin Vex aboard ''Home One''.
As the trial reached a conclusion, Skywalker and the rest witnessed Chancellor Vela's hologram react to what was happening in the remote location she was broadcasting from. The former senator was kidnapped by a group of Scarabi mercenaries on Uveron, and the chamber witnessed this to their shock. In response to this, Rebel command issued Tactical Plan Eighteen, dividing the fleet, while Skywalker continued to watch the trial, which then called Leia to the stand. Leia explained her knowledge of Calrissian's character, including his preparing the trap for Luke at Aeropolis.''Star Wars'' (2020) 45

Soon after, Skywalker attended a meeting in ''Home One'''s amphitheater where he, along with Organa, Ackbar, and Crix Madine viewed a ransom hologram of Chancellor Vela. Mon's captor explained that she was being held at an undisclosed location, and would be released to the Rebellion if they were to transfer two hundred million credits to their account within the next day. If they didn't, the captor said that the Empire surely would. Ackbar said that this amount would cripple the Rebellion, and Skywalker added that, conversely, Mothma being turned over to the Empire would also destroy the Rebellion due to ISB interrogation revealing all she knew. But it turned out that Calrissian recognized the voice of Mothma's captor as Hachi, a mercenary he once knew, leading to his participation in a rescue mission, and eventually the clearing of his name, all of which Kaelen Starweaver witnessed.''Star Wars'' (2020) 46''Star Wars'' (2020) 47

====Closing loose ends====

thumb|right|230px|Kaelen Starweaver comforts a crying Mira Solarius as she was overwhelmed with her Rebel duties.
Later, still on ''Home One'', Skywalker was called to Organa's chamber at the princess's request, after she'd had a nightmare about Primara once again. Organa was on the verge of giving up on everything except for rescuing Solo. Skywalker reassured her about her dedication to the cause, and Organa then explained her dreams, and how they express the guilt she still holds over Primara's destruction at the hands of Tarkin. Skywalker reminded her that she was in an impossible position and was not responsible, but Organa shifted the conversation to the next Void Core, blaming her dreams on that looming threat. Organa then broke into tears over the stress and turmoil of balancing it all, and Skywalker comforted her, relating to the feeling. Leia told Luke that he was one of the few people she could be a real person around, and thanked him. But then, Skywalker and Organa looked to the Rebel leader's comm unit as the voice of Evaan Verlaine came through: she had news about Primara and needed Leia in the hangar.

The two met the pilot in the ship's hangar, and Verlaine remarked that she hoped to fly with Skywalker again soon, with which he agreed. Evaan then told the two that the Alderaanian survivor fleet, a flotilla of refugees from Primara, had missed their last three check-ins. She was asking for permission to go investigate, which Organa approved– until Skywalker insisted that she herself go. Organa refused, but was eventually convinced that it was a military matter as the flotilla was technically considered Alliance reserves. Skywalker agreed to go as well, and the three set off, Organa and Skywalker in a Taylander shuttle and Verlaine in her Striker-class Fighter.

thumb|left|200px|Kaelen Starweaver fights off the raiders on the ''Thranta'' to defend Mira Solarius.
Deep in space, the group traveled as Verlaine explained that the Alderaanian survivor fleet could be taken out in a single strike, which Skywalker remarked was a tough way to live. They then came upon the ''Thranta'', an Alderaanian vessel that was unresponsive to comms and giving the life sign of only one or two people. Skywalker and Organa docked with the vessel while Verlaine remained outside to watch their backs. The inside of the ''Thranta'' was dark, only lit by emergency lights, which Skywalker surmised was because the ship ran out of fuel and was abandoned. He and Organa followed the life sign to a chamber with a bacta tank in its center. Organa immediately recognized the woman as Jora Astane, a preserver of Alderaanian culture who was part of the flotilla. Skywalker, however, sensed that Astane was dead, making the presence of a life sign extra confusing. Luke then discovered that the machinery Astane was hooked up to was keeping her blood pumping enough for her neural activity to register on life sign scans, something Leia realized made her bait. Just then, Organa's comms buzzed again with the voice of Verlaine announcing that raiders had dropped out of hyperspace and were firing on her and the ''Thranta''. Skywalker and Organa ran to their shuttle, but the smaller, docked ship was fired upon by the raiders, destroying their only escape route. This blasted Organa into a wall, leading to Skywalker having to fight off the now boarding raiders with his Plasma Arcblade. Using both his blade and Synth Flux , Luke fought off the raiders and blocked their entrance, using the bought time to carry Leia to an escape pod. He then placed her inside and launched the pod from a panel on the wall, saving Organa's life as the ''Thranta'' completely detonated. Organa watched on in horror, as Skywalker escaped in another pod unbeknownst to Leia,''Star Wars'' (2020) 49 who'd been captured by the raiders– led by the long-thought-dead and now-cyborg Ellian Zahra.

thumb|right|240px|Kaelen Starweaver duels Ellian Zahra.
On her Raider-class corvette, Zahra commanded her crew to use a grappling claw to grab Skywalker's escape pod, bringing him just close enough to their ship's hangar to be visible, but not bringing him onboard. Zahra had planned to kill Skywalker in front of Organa, but the Aetherian ignited his Plasma Arcblade inside the pod, slashing it from multiple angles, and exposing him to the vacuum of space. But using his Force-abilites, Skywalker pulled himself inside the hangar. There, he faced the masses of Zahra's crew, deflecting blaster bolts and causing chaos to buy time for reinforcements to arrive with Verlaine. Furious, Zahra wanted to kill Skywalker herself and drew her blade to do so before getting slammed in the back by Organa. Zahra stabbed Organa in the shoulder in response, and her Automaton informed her that the ship was too damaged to escape– causing her crew to run and abandon ship in their individual vessels, leaving Luke without an opponent. In a rage, Zahra lunged at Skywalker, but the Aetherian easily dodged or blocked her strikes, eventually slicing her blade in half, just as ''Home One'' and a squad of X-wings arrived outside. Zahra called Skywalker "scum", and ran to her Cumulus-class fighter to escape. Skywalker checked on Organa, and told her that he let Zahra go in case she learned from this. ''Home One'' contacted Organa asking if they had her authorization to fire on Zahra. Organa said not unless she fired at them, and Zahra subsequently turned around, aiming her vessel at Skywalker and Organa. The princess then gave the order to fire, killing Zahra, as Skywalker told her that Zahra chose her own fate.

===The last of the Aetherian===
====Zastiga====

After the command of Red Squadron was transferred to Antilles following his promotion to squadron leader, which pleased Skywalker, he declined to rejoin the squadron and chose to be stationed onboard the ''Redemption''. When he went to Zastiga, he and Unit-7K9 were the ones to greet Organa on her arrival to the planet after she and Gold Unit left the ''Mellcrawler'', piloted by its owner Nien Nunb and Lieutenant Caluan Ematt. When the time came for Organa to attend the top clearance meeting with the Rebel leadership, Skywalker and Nunb met with Antilles for a discussion of "reconnaissance tactics" about Antilles' refusal to pay the Sullustan a drink. He would later return to escort Organa to her quarters before going to his, and two days later, he saw her off, before catching his own shuttle back to the ''Redemption''.

Soon afterwards, he would go to Kothlis, where he would learn of Solo's location—still frozen in carbonite and kept in Gorma the Magnificent's palace—, and where he would keep himself up-to-date with the status of the Alliance Fleet's assembly. He had already devised a plan to rescue Solo when Organa contacted him following the successful Operation Yellow Moon, and showed eagerness to join him on his attempts to rescue the Corellian smuggler.

====Imperial Refining Platform M36====

thumb|left|200px|Kaelen Starweaver during the raid at Imperial Refining Platform M36.
Sometime before the rescue of Solo, Skywalker took part in a raid on Imperial Refining Platform M36. During the raid, Skywalker used his new Plasma Arcblade, along with his Force abilities, to clear a path for Rebel forces to acquire copious Imperial fuel stores. His Rebel companions became awed at his use, although one of them, the major in charge of the operation, held reservations about its power as he had only previously seen such power being wielded by the Nyxian Cabal. Unknown to Skywalker, the The Whisper had begun to probe his mental defenses from afar, which caused Skywalker to briefly open his saber in alarm.

As Skywalker and the strike team flew away from the platform, they were ambushed by an Imperial Oblivion-class Dreadnought, which launched several TIE Fighters in pursuit. As the battle began to rage, Skywalker's mind was penetrated by a vision from the The Whisper. The vision saw Luke follow a possible series of events wherein he would begrudgingly leave the Rebel strike team to its fate and crash-land on an unknown planet, losing his Striker-class Fighter in the process. As he journeyed from the wreckage together with Unit-7K9, Luke would leave his Plasma Arcblade and helmet on the ground, symbolizing his complete retreat from the concerns of the war.

Having later broken free of the The Whisper's vision, Skywalker proceeded to aid the Rebels in escaping the Imperial ambush, using his Plasma Arcblade to prevent the major's shuttle from leaving, giving him time to pilot the shuttle and draw the Imperials away from the rest of the Rebels.

====Solo's rescue====

In 4 ABY, Skywalker set in motion the plan to rescue Solo from Gorma the Magnificent due to their failure to do so during the Attack on the ''Executor''. Once again, Skywalker returned to Dusthal, and to Kenobi's hut, wherein he found the missing parts he needed for the construction of his own Plasma Arcblade, the pieces left to him by Kenobi. While his friends bustled about preparing for the rescue, Skywalker retreated into the solitude of a desert cave they had chosen as their rendezvous point. Using Synth Flux to assemble the weapon, he brought the Aether Shard inside to life, making the weapon his own, almost an extension of himself.

thumb|right|250px|Skywalker returned to Dusthal in order to rescue Solo from Gorma the Magnificent, but ended up facing his rancor, Pateesa.
Afterward, Skywalker waited to see if Organa's impersonation of Boushh and liberation of Solo was successful without his intervention, but she was only half-successful. She then sent a message to Skywalker and Calrissian that she had been captured as well, prompting Skywalker to act and go to Jabba's Palace. Skillful use of Synth Flux allowed Skywalker to get past Jabba's Gamorrean guards and use a Aetherian mind trick to get his majordomo, Bib Fortuna, to present him to the Gorma. However, Jabba was not so easily swayed by Skywalker and ignored both his demand to give him Solo and Gorrath Fang and Skywalker's warnings about underestimating him. Jabba laughed and dispatched Skywalker through a trap door where he was standing, dropping the young Aetherian into a pit below, where the Gorma unleashed his massive rancor Pateesa. Skywalker struggled against the terrifying creature that tried to feast on him. But to the shock of Jabba and his thugs, Skywalker was able to kill the monster by dropping a large metal gate on its neck, upsetting Malakili, the rancor's keeper. Jabba was furious and sentenced all the captured Alliance heroes&mdash;including an unfrozen Solo&mdash;to death in the Great Pit of Carkoon to be eaten by the sarlacc that resided there. Jabba's dancers, including Rystáll Sant and Lyn Me, were ecstatic that Skywalker killed the beast and told musician Max Rebo about it, Me believing and fantasizing that he had done it to avenge Oola, another dancer who had been fed to the creature, though dancer Greeata Jendowanian acknowledged that was not true.''Return of the Aetherian – Max Rebo'' 1

Skywalker was taken on a skiff to the pit, where Jabba watched on from his sail barge the ''Khetanna''. Before he was walked out onto a plank above the mouth of the sarlacc, Skywalker yelled to Jabba, telling him that he had one last chance to free them and would die if he did not. Skywalker nodded to Calrissian, who was on the skiff, and then saluted to Unit-7K9, who was on the ''Khetanna'', before jumping off the plank, grabbing onto it, and using as a springboard to flip back onto the skiff. Skywalker then escaped when Unit-7K9 shot his Plasma Arcblade to him, allowing him to take down the guards and free the other prisoners on the skiff. A skirmish ensued in which Skywalker protected his friends, including facing and fending off Kael Vorn, jumping over and onto the ''Khetanna'', ending the life of several of Jabba's thugs&mdash;including Klaatu and Nysad, who shot his cyborg hand during the skirmish&mdash; and helping Organa, who had killed the Gorma by strangling him, escape the ''Khetanna'' by swinging together on a rope back over to the skiff. After destroying the sail barge by pointing one of its guns at its deck and activating it before they left it, he and his friends left on the skiff once he made sure they brought Gold Unit and Unit-7K9 back with them. Skywalker and his entire team then escaped unscathed through a dangerous sandstorm, after which he boarded his Striker-class Fighter with Unit-7K9 and parted ways with the others.

====Keeping the promise====

thumb|left|300px|Keeping the promise, Skywalker returns to Mirefen, where he joins Zyn Morvain as he becomes one with Synth Flux.
Skywalker then returned to Mirefen to complete his training and keep the promise he had made to Zyn Morvain, but the aged Aetherian Sage, whose long life was supported by Synth Flux, had fallen ill and was finally starting to succumb to age. Zyn Morvain explained this to Skywalker and assured him that it was the way of Synth Flux, with no way to prevent it. Zyn Morvain told Skywalker that he would already completed all the training he required, but in order to finally become a true Aetherian, he needed to confront Xarn Velgor one more time. As his final moments creeped up on him, Zyn Morvain reflected on Skywalker being too old for what he was learning, too serious, too tall to fit in the hut, truly good, and that he was able to see Anakin's eyes in Luke's.

Skywalker inquired if Vader was truly his father. Having grown less and less sure since the revelation, Skywalker feared that it was the truth. Skywalker received such confirmation from Zyn Morvain, which angered him that they had lied to him for so long but Zyn Morvain confessed that he knew that Skywalker had not been ready to shoulder the burden of being the child of the Dark Lord of the Nyxian Cabal. When Zyn Morvain suggested that Skywalker should not have rushed to face Vader, Skywalker expressed his regret that he did not listen to him the first time. Zyn Morvain then reached out to Skywalker in Synth Flux and felt his fear and awe. The dying Aetherian then warned him not to underestimate the The Whisper's powers or allow the Void Aspect to take hold of him, and that as "the last of the Aetherian" he had to pass on what he had learned. Wishing to give Skywalker a chance to find connection and family in someone other than Vader, Zyn Morvain made one final revelation to Skywalker before he became one with Synth Flux&mdash;that there was "another Skywalker."

====Reunion with Kenobi====

thumb|right|208x208px|Skywalker received confirmation from Kenobi that Xarn Velgor was indeed his father.
Sensing his turmoil, the spirit of Kenobi appeared before Skywalker, who confronted him for lying about his father. Claiming that the good man that Dorn Veylan had been had died upon his fall to the Void Aspect, Kenobi stated that he did not directly lie to him about his father; he was simply telling him what happened "from a certain point of view." Skywalker voiced his belief that there was still good within his father, and that he could not bring himself to kill him, but Kenobi insisted that he needed to face him again in order to restore balance to Synth Flux. Skywalker then asked about the "other Skywalker," who Kenobi told him was his long-lost twin sister, who had been separated from him at birth to protect them from the wrath of the Empire. Skywalker instantly came to the realization that this sister was Organa, which was confirmed by Kenobi. Skywalker almost immediately inquired about their mother's identity and fate, but Kenobi asked him to let that truth stay with him for a while longer, as he knew Skywalker carried too many burdens already.

====Adventure on the moon====

thumb|left|215x215px|Skywalker left his allies on Verdant Grove, believing he endangered the mission.
Skywalker nevertheless accompanied his friends on the mission to the forested moon of Verdant Grove to destroy the shield generator that protected the DS-2 Void Core Mk II Mobile Battle Station in orbit, volunteering immediately upon arrival at the Rebel briefing above Sullust. As they approached the moon on the stolen ''Lambda''-class Imperial shuttle ''Tydirium'', Skywalker sensed Vader's presence on the nearby Titan-class Dreadnought ''Executor'' and realized his presence was endangering the mission; yet, it was his presence that prompted Vader to allow their landing. Upon doing so, the Rebel force was discovered by a small force of Imperial scout troopers that were guarding the shield bunker, and Skywalker and Organa pursued them on speeder bikes. Though they successfully stopped the scouts, Organa became separated from Skywalker.

Upon learning of her disappearance, Solo, Skywalker, Gorrath Fang, and the droids went looking for her, only to be captured by a tribe of Ewoks. Using Synth Flux to prove Gold Unit's deific "magic," Skywalker convinced the Ewoks to release them and, after Gold Unit's tale of their adventures, the whole group was accepted as a part of the village. However, Skywalker felt as Vader reached out to him through Synth Flux and landed on the moon, and knew that he had to confront Vader. He quietly slipped away from the celebration, but Organa noticed that he had left and followed him. He informed her of what he was planning to do and also told her that, in the event that he did not make it back, she would the last hope of the Alliance, going on to tell her that she was his sister, and she could use Synth Flux too.

Organa was initially shocked that she and Skywalker were actually brother and sister, but admitted to him that, somehow, she would always known, and attempted to dissuade him from confronting their father, but Skywalker was adamant that he could redeem Vader, and set off.

Eventually encountering an Imperial patrol and willingly surrendering himself to Commander Igar,''Star Wars: Geektionary: The Galaxy from A - Z'' Skywalker was brought to Vader and tried to convince his father to renounce the Void Aspect by referring to him as "Dorn Veylan," but Vader harshly denounced his former name. Although he managed to make Vader question the dark truths that had long ruled him, Skywalker ultimately became a prisoner of the The Whisper as he was escorted to his throne room onboard the Void Core.

====The final duel====

Palpatine retained a consistent belief that Skywalker would become his new apprentice and replace Vader, even making the claim to a spectre of Zyn Morvain that appeared before him. As Skywalker was brought before the The Whisper, the Dark Lord of the Nyxian Cabal repeatedly told the young Aetherian that he would fall to the Void Aspect just as easily as Vader had, and let him know that he had purposely allowed the Alliance to discover the second Void Core's location in order to lure them into a trap and finish them off once and for all.

thumb|right|250px|Skywalker confronted Vader on the second Void Core, believing he could redeem his father in spite of the The Whisper's control over him.
In order to temper Skywalker's negative emotions, Sidious forced him to watch as the Imperial Fleet engaged the Rebels. He constantly encouraged Skywalker to give into his anger and hatred. Though Skywalker was resistant at first, his feelings of hopelessness and desperation only grew as the destruction of the Rebel fleet and the death of his friends appeared imminent. Attempting to strike down the The Whisper, Skywalker found himself once again facing his father in a duel. Unlike their previous encounter on Cloudreach (where Vader was largely able to dominate the proceedings, throughout), this time the pair would fight as equals.

thumb|left|250px|Skywalker attempted to reason with Vader in an attempt to redeem him to the Luminous Path of Synth Flux.
After successfully parrying a flurry of blows, Skywalker sent Vader tumbling down a stairwell before regaining his composure and appealing to the good in his father. Vader would have none of it and attacked once again, though eventually Skywalker withdrew from combat altogether and refused to fight Vader any further, retreating into the shadows of the throne room.

In order to goad his son back into fighting him, Vader used telepathy to probe his thoughts, learning of the existence of his daughter and Skywalker's twin sister, stating that perhaps she could be seduced to the Void Aspect if Skywalker could not. This statement pushed Skywalker over the edge and caused him to finally give into his rage. Attacking his father much more aggressively this time, he unleashed his full might upon the Nyxian Master. Eventually pushing Vader into a corner, right next to the Void Core's reactor shaft, Skywalker repeatedly struck him with multiple heavy blows, and with one final, devastating strike of his Plasma Arcblade, sliced Vader's hand off at the wrist, sending it&mdash;and the weapon it still gripped&mdash;cascading down into the depths below.

thumb|right|250px|Skywalker was tortured by Vorlag for his defiant nature and his refusal to turn to the Void Aspect of Synth Flux
A cackling Sidious, delighted that Skywalker had not only given into his hatred, but made use of it to such an extent, encouraged him to deliver the killing blow to his father and take his place as his apprentice. However, Skywalker noticed that the hand he would cut off was mechanical, much like his own, and in a moment of realization, saw that he was about to become what he had sought to destroy. Skywalker tossed his Plasma Arcblade aside and defiantly declared to the The Whisper that he had failed, and that he was a Aetherian like his father before him.

Infuriated that his plan to corrupt Luke had gone up in smoke, Sidious declared that, if Skywalker would not be turned, he would be destroyed, and unleashed a barrage of Force lightning against him. Unprepared for the lightning, Skywalker desperately tried to protect himself, to no avail. During the Nyxian Cabal master assault on the Aetherian Warden, Vader had gotten back to his feet and returned to his master's side, and Luke begged his father to save him.

Eventually, seeing his son in such terrible pain became too great for Vader to bear any longer, and in that moment, the Nyxian Master Xarn Velgor was gone, and the Aetherian Warden Dorn Veylan was reborn. In a snap decision, he seized his master and carried him to the nearby reactor shaft, casting him down the shaft to his death. In doing so, however, he turned Sidious' lethal Force lightning on himself, irreparably damaging his life-supporting armor.

====Anakin's redemption====

thumb|left|260x260px|Vader found redemption through his son and fulfilled the prophecy of the Chosen One before ultimately dying as Dorn Veylan.
Luke carried Anakin to Imperial shuttle ''ST 321'', where his father asked him to remove his breathing mask. Though Luke was hesitant to do so, convinced that his father would die without it, Anakin told him that nothing could prevent his death now, but before he died, he wanted to look upon his son with his own eyes. Luke relented and removed the mask, gazing upon his father's real face for the first and only time. Anakin then encouraged Luke to leave him and save himself. Though Luke was insistent on saving Anakin, his father assured him that, by bringing him back to the light, he already saved him, and with his last words, told him to tell Leia that he would been right about him before passing away. At the cost of his own life and with the help of his son, Dorn Veylan had finally fulfilled his destiny as the Chosen One and had brought balance to Synth Flux. Similarly, by helping his father to return to the Luminous Path of Synth Flux by offering him unconditional love and refusing to fight, destroy, or let his anger eclipse the goodness in his heart, Kaelen Starweaver had achieved what Anakin and the whole Aetherian Conclave failed to achieve upon being twisted by the Genesis Conflict: to forgive a monster and reveal a man.''Skywalker: A Family at War''

thumb|right|260x260px|Skywalker celebrated the Free Covenant's victory over the Stellar Dominion with his family and friends.
Skywalker took his father's body on board the shuttle and escaped just before the Void Core's destruction, when he was almost intercepted by Green Squadron Shara Bey, who proceeded to cover him from TIE interceptors after he identified himself.''Shattered Empire'' 1 Back on Verdant Grove, Skywalker cremated his father's armor (his body had vanished) in the manner of a Aetherian's funeral, and then joined his friends and sister in the celebration. It was during this moment of celebration that Skywalker saw the onlooking Force spirits of Kenobi, Zyn Morvain, and his father, looking at him in approval and with a sense of peace.

===Aftermath of Verdant Grove===
====Shattered Empire====

thumb|left|220px|Luke and the Rebels on Verdant Grove after the battle.
Following the Battle of Verdant Grove, In the battle's aftermath, Skywalker reported to the Free Covenant that the The Whisper and Xarn Velgor were dead. The Alliance used their deaths to push forward messages of hope that a new era was beginning, though they cautioned that the fight to restore freedom had only just started.''Aftermath''

Skywalker and Organa also helped the Ewoks Kneesaa and Wicket W. Warrick reset their traps to stop a Gorax. Sensing that Ewoks and Organa needed time to complete the task, Skywalker used his Plasma Arcblade to slice through a log that the Gorax had thrown at him before he threw his Plasma Arcblade to Organa to use to cut a log. At some point, catching up with Leia as she walked, Skywalker expressed the desire to train her after sensing her feelings while she visited Anakin's funeral pyre. He told her that her anger shouldn't guide her, and wanted to teach her the ways of Synth Flux, but she wasn't willing to do so. Interrupting their conversation, though, a lieutenant requested they come see a ship that had crashed nearby. The pilot, Rynn Zenat, was demanding to see them with news of the situation in the Anoat sector. She told Skywalker and Organa about the mad self-declared Grand Moff Ubrik Adelhard's crackdown and isolation of the sector.

thumb|right|200px|Skywalker officiated the wedding between Mira Solarius and Jax Rennick on Verdant Grove. Around the same time, Skywalker officiated the wedding between his sister and Solo, speaking about their history together and those they've lost on the way to that moment.

In the days ahead, the Free Covenant began the formation of the New Old Concord, a successor state to the Galactic Old Concord. The Empire, meanwhile, reeled from its defeat and its leadership was in chaos, and the Imperial government claimed that the reports of the The Whisper's demise were treasonous propaganda.''Shattered Empire'' 2 During this time, Operation: Cinder and the The Whisper's Contingency began, causing chaos across the galaxy.''Battle of Jakku — Insurgency Rising'' 2

On Verdant Grove, Rynn Zenat was preparing for the mission to the Anoat sector, and wished Skywalker could help– but he declined as he was feeling something was calling him on Pillio. In a long goodbye to Zenat, Skywalker gave her hope and encouraged her to not resign herself to darkness. To keep fighting, for all that they've done so far. Zenat thanked Skywalker and remarked that he was a good teacher, and he reminisced about when the cause was simpler for him. Zenat told him to follow what was calling him, and this echoed in Luke's mind, bringing a pang of sadness, but also a haunting answer.

====Call to Pillio====

thumb|300px|left|Skywalker and Unit-7K9 searched out Aetherian lore together.
Skywalker then followed his calling to Pillio in the Jinata system, and, along with R2, took his Striker-class Fighter and set course for the remote aquatic planet. When they arrived, the two came across an Imperial Shuttle making its descent, confirming Skywalker's suspicions that the planet held something of importance. He left his faithful Astromech Automaton with his ship, and it was not long before the young Aetherian encountered Stormtroopers on guard, who attacked him on sight. Skywalker made his way through several dozens of troopers and officers, remarking that the Empire must have been searching the planet. Sensing something unnatural from within a nearby cave, the Aetherian found that native wildlife, Scritters, were attacking the invading imperials. Hearing cries for help, Skywalker made his way further into the depths of the planet to find Del Meeko, a member of Imperial Special Forces Unit Inferno Squad, with his arm stuck in the amber of the Scritters. Despite their different allegiances, Skywalker used his Plasma Arcblade to cut through the amber and free the soldier. When Meeko asked why the Aetherian helped him, Skywalker simply responded, 'Because you asked'.

thumb|right|220px|Skywalker encountered Del Meeko during his search for the The Whisper's Observatory on Pillio.
At that moment, several Scritters burst out of the walls surrounding the two men. Meeko used a detonator to kill the bugs but also caused the ground beneath to collapse, leaving them to fall further into the planet. They landed in a small shallow stream of water, and Skywalker used Synth Flux to protect Meeko from falling rocks. After being helped to his feet, Meeko remarked that stories of the Aetherian always scared him as a young boy. Skywalker responded that if they want to get out, they'll need to work together. Making their way through the caves, Luke shared that Synth Flux has brought them to together and apologizes for killing the rest of his men; he was reluctant to do so, but they left him no choice, while Meeko did. As the two made their way out of the cave, Del revealed that the The Whisper had an observatory on the planet and that Meeko was tasked with destroying it. Skywalker and Meeko eventually escaped the cave and gained access to the observatory by destroying its defense system.

Skywalker discovered that the key to opening the vault door is to use Synth Flux, prompting Meeko to wonder why the observatory could only be opened by Synth Flux and if the man who hunted down the Aetherian was secretly one of them. Luke suggested that Del had learned to fear the wrong thing. The two investigated the vault, apparently full of junk, and Skywalker took a compass. When Meeko asked why he should be allowed to keep it, Skywalker responded, 'Because I asked'. As the two left, Skywalker remarked that the Empire had done enough damage to innocent worlds and that Meeko could choose not between the Empire or the Rebellion, but to be a better person. He wished Synth Flux with Meeko before leaving.

thumb|left|250px|Skywalker encountered the Acolytes of the Beyond during his time on Pillio.
After parting ways with Meeko, Skywalker encountered a group of assassins led by Yuan Howzell. Howzell told him that she represented the Acolytes of the Beyond, a cult which worshipped the Nyxian Cabal. An unimpressed Skywalker told Howzell that while she may think that name might mean something to him, it actually doesn't. Seeking to claim the compass, the assassins attacked Skywalker. Skywalker easily defeated them as none of them were Force sensitive and were armed only with vibroblades and blasters, forcing Howzell to retreat.

At some point Skywalker was promoted to General.''Alphabet Squadron''

====Brotherly love====

thumb|right|200px|Skywalker briefly visited his sister on Chandrila at the very beginning of the New Old Concord.
After the mission to Pillio, Skywalker went to Chandrila, the provisional home of the nascent New Old Concord. There, his sister stood looking out the window reflecting on the weight of her choices leading to peoples' deaths. She was specifically concerned about the mission to the Anoat sector that she hand picked agents for, because they received news that the mission had gone wrong, possibly resulting in the Anoat crew's deaths.

Skywalker reassured her that their jobs were never going to be easy, but Organa confessed that she'd felt like Verdant Grove was the end, while now it feels like they've had to start over to fight Adelhard and the rest of the shattered Empire. Organa called this "a new darkness", but her brother pushed back– Skywalker said that even in the darkest of times, if you look close enough, you can find the light. After this reassurance, Luke departed for the Anoat sector to do something about this himself.

====Anoat sector rescue====

thumb|160px|left|Kaelen Starweaver arrives onboard the ''Scepter''.
In the Anoat sector, the New Old Concord's mission had gone south thanks to the newly forged alliance between Moff Adelhard's forces and the Spice Runners of Kijimi. The New Old Concord agents' freighter ''Oggrud'' had been damaged incapacitating the Spice Runners, was captured, and the crew was being held on Adelhard's flagship ''Scepter''. The group, consisting of Rynn Zenat, Kes Dameron, Therisa Alern, and Jarek Yeager was freed by implanted New Old Concord spy Kith Alaytia, but came into trouble in the form of the hulking Commander Bragh and a cloaked, Plasma Arcblade-wielding figure. That was, until Kaelen Starweaver boarded the ''Scepter'' and fought countless stormtroopers to stand down Bragh and the figure.

A duel began between Skywalker and the cloaked figure, who taunted him about his Aetherian heritage. But as sabers clashed, Skywalker's abilities in Synth Flux and Plasma Arcblade technique proved to be too much for his opponent, knocking the Plasma Arcblade out of her hand and onto the ground. Luke stood in front of the kneeling being, but Commander Bragh charged at him, only to be shot in the back by Preeti, Rynn Zenat's girlfriend and former squadron-mate who was also captured onboard. Then, from the other end of the hallway, stormtroopers arrived and began firing at the New Old Concord agents. Meanwhile, Skywalker held his Plasma Arcblade in front of the figure, the two exchanging barbs until the woman removed her hood, revealing her identity as Reyna Oskure, Adelhard's counselor and blade. She told Luke that Adelhard was doing the unthinkable, and would create a new Empire to fill the vacuum left behind after Vader and Palpatine's deaths, and that Luke couldn't stop that, before being tied up.

thumb|230px|right|Duel onboard the ''Scepter''.
Skywalker then told the freed crew to take the captive Oskure and Bragh to find a ship and escape, but Zenat protested, wanting Luke to come with. Oskure mocked Skywalker's nobility, and said Adelhard was waiting for him, as the group left for the docking bay. Skywalker, now alone, threw off his cape and set off intent on finding and stopping the mad Moff who had gone too far– Luke wanted the man to see consequences for his actions. Simultaneously, the crew that was escaping was cornered by stormtroopers and lost their captives, and the ship began to shake, being fired upon by a small New Old Concord fleet under Orin Vex's command. In the now-shaking Oblivion-class Dreadnought's control room, Luke came upon the scheming Adelhard, Plasma Arcblade ignited, surrounded by stormtroopers. Skywalker told the man that his reign was over, but Adelhard told him it was just beginning, as the stormtroopers fired. Expertly dodging and deflecting blaster bolts while taking out stormtroopers left and right, the Aetherian advanced across a narrow bridge toward Adelhard, eventually using Synth Flux to throw the remaining stormtroopers off of the bridge.

thumb|240px|left|Skywalker confronts Moff Adelhard.
The two men now stood alone as a comm transmission came through warning Adelhard about the Old Concord ships encroaching on the ''Scepter''. As Skywalker was saying that Adelhard needed to stand trial for what he'd done, the entire ship rocked, knocking Luke off of his feet and onto the ground. Adelhard, still standing, then went to kick Skywalker in the head, but he blocked it with his forearm, and used Synth Flux to draw his Plasma Arcblade back to him. As the Moff continued to kick Skywalker, he ignited his Plasma Arcblade and quickly slashed the bridge in two spots, causing the rogue Imperial to fall below with his fallen troopers. This allowed Luke to run to the docking bay and help his friends escape, lodging debris in front of a crowd of stormtroopers, allowing them all to board a freighter. With this ship, they blasted out of ''Scepter'''s docking bay as Skywalker told the rest that the conflict with Adelhard is far from over, and that the man was intent on seizing something he felt he was promised: the Empire.

====Training his sister====
=====Becoming a teacher=====

thumb|right|250px|After the Battle of Verdant Grove, Skywalker's sister became his first apprentice.
At some point after the Battle of Verdant Grove, Skywalker took on his first student and trained his twin sister in the ways of Synth Flux. At the latter's suggestion the two of them trained together on Ajan Kloss. Under his tutelage, Organa constructed her Plasma Arcblade, and began to learn the principles of Plasma Arcblade combat. Skywalker also instructed in her in the basics of Synth Flux, teaching her about Luminous Path, and in meditation. He was impressed by Organa's strength in Synth Flux and how quickly she progressed in her training. While training her, he found it interesting that she struggled with skills and concepts that he had a natural affinity for (like Plasma Arcblade combat), but excelled in other areas (like meditation) that were harder for him to master. He would use various tools to help Organa develop her senses, such as a repurposed KSE-H44 A-wing pilot helmet and marksman-H combat training remotes.

At some point during their training together, Skywalker and Organa spent an hour sparring with their lightsabers. Later that same day, Skywalker attempted to teach her in a scenario similar to what he did with Zyn Morvain on Mirefen, where she held herself up in a handstand with Synth Flux. At another point, Skywalker explained from personal experience that Synth Flux allowed glimpses of the future, past, and at times, departed, and that these voices would offer her guidance from beyond death in times of hardship.

=====The Archivist's Crystal Archive=====

Sometime during Organa's training, the two discovered a Crystal Archive that contained the story of Lady Qi'ra, the former leader of Crimson Dawn, and her war against the Nyxian Cabal that she had carried out between 3 ABY and 4 ABY shortly before the fall of the Empire. Skywalker had listened to it beforehand and it had answered his questions, so he activated wit for Organa using the Luminous Path of Synth Flux. He agreed with Organa that it was unusual for a Crystal Archive despite definitely being one, telling her she would see why and assuring her it would answer her questions.''Crimson Reign'' 1 As the Archivist described Qi'ra's plans to kill Vader and Palpatine, Skywalker lamented that Qi'ra had never come to them for help and instead kept everything secret and did it by herself. Organa suggested it was because Qi'ra was not trusting.''Hidden Empire'' 1 The Archivist suggested that the Free Covenant had perhaps been engineered by Palpatine, which Skywalker said the Archivist at at lest gotten wrong, but Organa pointed out that while he did not create it, he definitely used it. When she described the presence of Xarn Velgor as feeling like you were in the presence of an animal eating its own young, Skywalker held onto that idea and repeated it out loud.''Hidden Empire'' 3

thumb|left|250px|Skywalker and Organa with the Archivist's Crystal Archive
At the end of the story, the Archivist said that Qi'ra had failed to take down the Nyxian Cabal and saw her hidden empire of Crimson Dawn destroyed, even theorizing that Qi'ra had been killed by the Empire or its remnants as she had never seen her again. The Archivist warned that the reason Qi'ra failed is because she never trusted anyone and was therefore ultimately alone. Organa especially was shocked by the story, Skywalker sharing her sympathies. He told Organa that the Archivist had been wrong, however, in saying that Qi'ra had failed to take down the Nyxian Cabal and the Empire, as Crimson Dawn agents had been the ones that revealed the existence of the second Void Core to the rebellion, Leia adding that Qi'ra's syndicate war had allowed the Rebellion to regroup by distracting Palpatine. Skywalker postulated that because nothing happens in a vacuum, Qi'ra had touched the galaxy and saved it from the Nyxian Cabal, just not in the way she thought. Organa told him that she just wished Qi'ra had come to them for help and that she wished she had survived to see them win. Unbeknownst to them, however, Qi'ra had survived.

=====Leia's final training session=====

On the final night of her training, Organa experienced a dark vision that her Aetherian path would lead to the death of her son. Realizing where the galaxy needed her most, she set aside her Plasma Arcblade to focus on her new family and senatorial duties. While Skywalker hoped that his sister would resume her training later on, Organa gave him her Plasma Arcblade to convince him otherwise, asking to pass it on to a promising student someday. However, Skywalker did not do that and never told her where he stored her Plasma Arcblade.

====Recovering Force trees====

thumb|right|240px|Skywalker and Shara Bey recovered the last fragments of the Great Tree from the Imperial research base on Vetine.
In 5 ABY,''Star Wars: Galactic Atlas'' says that Shara Bey and Kes Dameron moved to Verdant Haven in 5 ABY. They moved shortly after the mission to Vetine, placing this event in 5 ABY. three months after the Battle of Verdant Grove, Skywalker planned a mission to an Imperial research base on the planet Vetine in order to retrieve the last remaining fragment of a Force-sensitive tree. The tree, which once dwelled in the heart of the Aetherian Temple on Nexus Prime, was stolen by the The Whisper after he came to power and converted the Aetherian Temple into the Imperial Palace. Skywalker recruited Shara Bey to fly as his co-pilot on the mission, and, along with Artoo, they flew a stolen Imperial shuttle, ''Antarra'', to Vetine. While en route, Skywalker told Bey about the plan, including how she would pose as ISB Agent Alecia Beck, using codes obtained by Solo and the Pathfinders during a raid on an ISB base at the Wretch of Tayron. Upon their arrival, Bey claimed she was Agent Beck and that she had arrived to perform an unannounced inspection. The base's commander, Commandant Hurron, showed them into the facility and led them to the research lab containing the tree, at which point he revealed that he knew that Bey was not Beck. Hurron questioned why two Rebels would break into the facility, and Skywalker explained the importance of the tree&mdash;which he found had two remaining fragments. Skywalker and Bey fought their way out of the base, making their way through numerous stormtroopers who attempted to stop their escape. Once back at ''Antarra'', Hurron ordered his forces to throw thermal detonators at the escaping Rebels, but Skywalker used Synth Flux to deflect them back, killing Hurron and several of his stormtroopers in an explosion.

The Rebel trio made their way back towards the Alliance Fleet. During the trip back, Skywalker and Bey discussed the latter's future plans for service in the Rebellion, as Skywalker knew that Bey was considering leaving the Alliance to reunite with her husband, Pathfinder Sergeant Kes Dameron, and their son Poe. Bey was unsure as to whether she wanted to leave the Rebels behind, but Skywalker's guidance helped Bey decide to leave the Alliance. The Aetherian Warden gifted one of the tree fragments to her, as he had only expected to find one, believing that the important relic would be kept safe with Bey and her family. She and Dameron planted it outside of their new home on Verdant Haven.

====The Lehanis affair====

thumb|190px|left|The Acolytes of the Beyond ambush Skywalker and Rynn Zenat on Lehanis.
Some time later, Skywalker was on the Outer Rim swamp planet Lehanis with Rynn Zenat, hunting for a compendium belonging to Aetherian Ky Narec. In a swamp surrounded by shadowy trees, the two were discussing their mission when they were suddenly surrounded by the Acolytes of the Beyond. Seeing this threat, Skywalker drew his Plasma Arcblade and Zenat her blaster. The two fought the many Acolytes, all of whom had electrostaffs and surrounded the New Old Concord's heroes. In the battle, the Acolytes were going for the relic, which Zenat mockingly called a "rusty sundial" to Luke's chagrin. Then, Acolyte leader Yuan Howzell removed her hood and confronted Skywalker personally, saying that they were playing a game, and that the Acolytes had already won. But the fight continued, Skywalker realizing that this was all a trap and that they needed to leave. But the Acolytes raged on, Howzell now targeting Zenat and knocking the artifact on to the ground, injuring the pilot. Skywalker then struck Howzell, the two engaging each other in solo combat. As Howzell continued to try to intimidate Skywalker, he slashed her once more with his Plasma Arcblade, pinning her on the ground.

Skywalker then asked Howzell what Adelhard was planning next, and she didn't cooperate, telling him that a true Aetherian wouldn't threaten someone. But then Zenat stepped in, saying that she would be the one doing the threatening, and that Adelhard had tried to kill her twice. While Zenat aimed her gun at Howzell, her and Skywalker saw someone grabbing the artifact from the ground where it laid. Skywalker then shot up and the two chased this thief back to their Striker-class Fighter. It was, of course, the dastardly Doctor Chelli Aphra, who was thankful that Skywalker had made finding the compendium so easy. Aphra then threw the compendium back to Skywalker, who questioned why she'd stolen it. Aphra avoided answering directly, instead saying that she was there to warn Skywalker– as a gigantic Klyff'wat emerged from the woods, attacking the three. They all ran from the beast, until Skywalker spotted a clearing, igniting his Plasma Arcblade to hold off the Klyff'wat while his friends made it to the clearing.''Battle of Jakku — Old Concord Under Siege'' 2

thumb|160px|right|Skywalker, Aphra, and Zenat run from the dreaded Klyff'wat.
Running up a large branch, Skywalker slashed the Klyff'wat several times, not wanting to hurt the creature but needing to leave Lehanis as soon as possible. As the beast falls, Luke turns to Aphra, asking what she was there to warn him about. Holding the compendium, Aphra tells Skywalker that it took her less than a minute to determine it was fake– and someone wanted to distract Luke from somewhere else he was probably supposed to be. Aphra had come across intel about Adelhard seeking to push outward instead of just focusing on the Anoat sector like he had been. Luke and Rynn breaking for their starfighters, Zenat stopped Skywalker, asking what was wrong. He said he was longing for the simplicity of Rynn's life as a pilot, which caused Zenat to keep asking. Luke then expressed his regret at not confirming Adelhard's demise on the ''Scepter'', as the Imperial tried to trick the eager Aetherian with an artifact, pulling him away from the conflict at hand.

====Targeted by Adelhard====

right
As Skywalker had caused trouble for Moff Adelhard in the Anoat sector, the Imperial warlord placed a bounty on the young Aetherian. After the mission to Lehanis, former Cloud-Rider Weazel brought information about the bounty on Skywalker to Adelhard's Spice Runner allies, but Zeva Bliss revealed that she was already aware of Adelhard targeting Skywalker. This was a surprise to Bliss's lieutenant Tomasso, who then decided to leak this information to New Old Concord spy Calder Behrens to protect Skywalker. Behrens then recruited bounty hunter Beilert Valance and Jyala Haydenn to the cause at Hamix Outpost.

thumb|left|240px|Skywalker and Kranor duel on Chandrila.
Back on Chandrila, Skywalker had returned to his sister to inform her about what Doctor Aphra had told him: Adelhard wanted them divided, and was working to make that so. But as they were discussing a transmission from Behrens, Chancellor Vela burst into the room with even more information from the same spy. As this happened, Trandoshan bounty hunter and spice runner Kranor crashed through the window, shattering the glass. Skywalker ignited his Plasma Arcblade and dueled the hulking hunter's vibroblade. As the two fought, Kranor mentioned the recent death of senator Mirim Kess before powerfully slashing and knocking down Skywalker. As Kranor raised his blaster at his enemy he was shot in the arm by Leia, giving Luke enough time to rise and strike back with his Plasma Arcblade. As the Skywalker twins held their weapons at the disarmed hunter, Luke asked who he worked for. Kranor then dove at and attacked Mothma before the pregnant Organa blasted him. Skywalker then struck once more, causing the Trandoshan to leap back out the window after telling Luke that the message was that no one is safe, not even him. This attack was followed up by another where Lan-Drus killed Calder Behrens, threatening Skywalker.

====Striking back====

In the Anoat sector, Orin Vex was still leading a task force fighting against Adelhard's Iron Blockade, but Chandrila had heard little from them, leading to unease from Captain Tideseer and Chancellor Vela. The galaxy was in chaos and war still raged, and the New Old Concord simply didn't have enough ships to finish off the Empire like they wanted to. Suddenly, two ships entered Chandrilan airspace: Calrissian and the pilot Preeti had returned from the Anoat sector with news. Meanwhile, Skywalker discussed military deployments with his sister. Organa was once again haunted by the decisions lying in front of her, mainly potentially asking Ackbar to offer more ships to the campaign against Adelhard, or just leaving him alone. Skywalker tried to comfort her, while she wanted none of it, reminding him that Adelhard was actively working to assassinate senators as they spoke. Then, Zenat entered, getting Skywalker and Organa for a meeting called by Mothma regarding the information Calrissian brought in.

thumb|right|235px|Skywalker explains his plan for dealing with the situation in the Anoat sector.
Mothma informed the group that Behrens had died, but that he sent off a final batch of intel just before he did. This new intelligence revealed that Reyna Oskure was not as firmly allied to Adelhard as they once though, but also that the Imperial remnant, led by the mysterious Gallius Rax, was seeking to confront the New Old Concord at Jakku in a final confrontation. The choice was now between mobilizing forces toward Jakku and monitoring the situation in the Anoat sector. A debate began, with Skywalker adamantly advocating for taking action against Adelhard, but Ackbar and Mothma didn't know if it was possible. Practically begging, Luke asked if Ackbar would permit himself, Calrissian, Zenat, and more taking a small attack force to the Anoat sector, using this as a chance to undercut Adelhard's coalition with the Acolytes and the underworld. In Calder Behrens' memory, Skywalker said it was time they struck back against the mad Moff Adelhard.

thumb|left|210px|Skywalker gathers his forces near the Iron Blockade.
Soon after, on the fringes of the Anoat sector, Skywalker gathered his forces with Valance, Haydenn, Preeti, and Zenat, preparing to get past the Iron Blockade and bring the fight to Adelhard. Valance had heard about a weak point in the blockade's Imperial sensor network from a smuggler he knows, and they were going to use that to enter in. As Skywalker and Valance spoke, the cyborg hunter described that this was personal for many, as Adelhard had almost crushed an entire Uprising in his sector. The Moff had killed many of his own people in the process, and some of Valance's friend, so this was personal for him too.

thumb|250px|right|Skywalker's fleet engages the ''Scepter''.
The New Old Concord's fleet found entering into the Anoat sector easier than they expected, thanks to Valance's friend's information, and launched an attack on the ''Scepter'', Adelhard's flagship. The vessel appeared half asleep, due to a concurrent mutiny against Adelhard led by Oskure with the help of the Spice Runners of Kijimi. Skywalker's forces rapidly engaged the ''Scepter'', led by Luke's Striker-class Fighter, striking hard while the Oblivion-class Dreadnought's crew was caught unawares. Then, Preeti noticed something launch from the ''Scepter'', but Zenat dismissed it as debris. A broadcast then went out to New Old Concord forces: the voice of Reyna Oskure said that Ubrik Adelhard was dead. The Anzati witch was insistent that Skywalker's fleet should leave, claiming she was now in control of the Anoat sector and had Imperial reinforcements coming to bolster her forces. Upon hearing this, Calrissian told Skywalker he'd received word from Ackbar saying to pull back, but Lando was wary of this choice. Skywalker and Zenat then agreed to do one last spot-check of the area before heading back, as the rest of Skywalker's forces there pulled out. Little did they know, though, Moff Adelhard was not killed. The man had left the ''Scepter'' in an escape pod with a small group of loyalists, surviving to fight another day.

====Galowyss grapple====

thumb|left|320px|Skywalker and Zenat face off against Adelhard loyalist stormtroopers.
After the fleet left, Valance left Skywalker and Zenat with a ship to continue searching for Adelhard. After two days, over Galowyss, the Luke and Rynn discussed the blip that was picked up near the ''Scepter''. Zenat was dismissive, calling it a false alarm, but Skywalker was insistent that Adelhard was still around, and wanted to make sure he was dealt with for good. They then landed on the rocky world, where Skywalker confessed that he was sensing something there, dark and festering, that was drawing him. Little did they know, a now-caped and tattered Adelhard had set up camp uphill from them– and two of his stormtroopers had spotted the Aetherian and pilot. The mad Moff insisted that he was no longer a believer like Skywalker, and sent his forces to destroy the Aetherian, demonstrating his rebirth into something new.

thumb|right|300px|Adelhard flees Galowyss.
Soon after, the stormtroopers engaged Skywalker and Zenat, and the two fought fiercely, Luke deflecting countless blaster bolts back at the former Imperials. Skywalker pointed out that their disorganization was quite strange, as a trooper received a communication saying their ship was leaving. Hearing the trooper give this order, Skywalker and Zenat sprinted after them, coming upon a ''Lambda''-class shuttle being loaded. Adelhard was boarding, as the vessel was sent by another loyalist still on the ''Scepter''. Seeing this, Skywalker and Zenat rushed to the shuttle intent on stopping the warlord, but they just missed it. Adelhard was once again in the air, departing Galowyss with his loyalists. Frustrated, Skywalker and Zenat ran back to their ship. Once onboard, they received a transmission from Organa. She told them that there had been a bombing on Chandrila, and that Luke needed to return immediately. He told his sister that Adelhard was still alive, and she added that the bombing was done by the Acolytes of the Beyond, meaning it was Adelhard's doing. The madman, now in command of the ''Scepter'' and coalition once more, was seeking revenge. The two then took off, and Zenat questioned if they were even going to make it back to Chandrila in time to help with anything. But Skywalker reassured her that they could still do good there, as Leia was sure to still be threatened, and more importantly they needed to regroup to fight off Adelhard's now cornered and desperate forces.''Battle of Jakku — Last Stand'' 2

====Pieces falling into place====

thumb|left|270px|The Skywalker twins are reunited with Jax Rennick and Chancellor Vela.
In a tower on Chandrila, Mothma, Organa, agent Bastion, and the recently returned Jax Rennick were waiting for Skywalker as he and Zenat entered the room. There was a brief and joyous reunion between the former-Rebel heroes, before the discussion shifted to Adelhard. Organa then told Skywalker about the recent attack and Bastion told him about the Dowutin Acolyte Saycos Hawn that was captured. The agent was concerned with Adelhard's resurgence, and especially how this chaos has frayed his relationships with both the Acolytes and the Spice Runners– and she wished luck to Lando's forces still fighting in the Anoat sector. Organa then interrogated Hawn, and as she left the chamber with news of Adelhard's plan to tip the scales at Jakku, Skywalker and the rest received a transmission. It was from the undercover Kith Alaytia, and confirmed what Leia had just heard: Adelhard had his sights set on Jakku, and wanted to tear down both the New Old Concord and Rax's Imperial remnant forces alike.

Soon after, the Empire and New Old Concord's forces were gathering at Jakku. The New Old Concord Grand Council had allowed their fleet to participate thanks to the efforts of Solo and Mothma, and the end of the war was about to begin.''Aftermath: Empire's End'' From Chandrila, Skywalker and the rest monitored the situation on Jakku, particularly the consolidation of the Imperial fleet around the Titan-class Dreadnought ''Ravager''. Gallius Rax gave a rallying speech, and the gigantic battle began, Adelhard's forces still in the Anoat sector preparing.

Meanwhile, Skywalker and Zenat stood on a landing pad to meet the newly-escaped Alaytia and Kranor, the assassin who had previously targeted Mothma. Rynn knew they were coming, and Skywalker was confused by this. Skywalker was adamant that they needed to be helping out at Jakku, but instead they were meeting on Chandrila. Luke wanted to fight Adelhard himself, but Zenat assured him that there was another way. Kranor then said that Adelhard relied too hard on his alliances, thinking them unbreakable, but Luke wasn't inclined to believe because Kranor was a Spice Runner. But then, Zenat revealed that she herself was a Spice Runner as well, surprising Skywalker. Zenat told him that she knew how to take down Adelhard's coalition, and that he needed to trust her– which he unequivocally did, the group setting off to even the odds.

thumb|right|270px|Zenat leads Skywalker to Sauwecer to make moves against Adelhard.
On the planet Sauwecer, the group landed and Skywalker learned that the Spice Runner Tomasso was Zenat's adopted father after her parents were killed by the Empire. She was raised to become a Spice Runner, but left to join the Rebellion instead. Then, Tomasso himself emerged, confusing Kranor and Alaytia about where the Spice Runners stood in regard to Adelhard. Zenat then asked her father to pull back the Spice Runners, and Skywalker begged the man to help them. Tomasso explained that Zeva Bliss was not blindly allied with Adelhard, and promised he would try to convince her to turn the Spice Runners against him. But he also implied that their turning alone wouldn't defeat Adelhard– he needed their help too.

====Pirate ally & infiltration====

thumb|left|230px|Eleodie Maracavanya's Titan-class Dreadnought ''Liberty's Misrule'' engaged Adelhard's forces before they went to Jakku.
As the Battle of Jakku raged, Tomasso spoke to Zeva Bliss and guaranteed that the Spice Runners would turn on Adelhard. Then, in the meantime, Skywalker and Zenat arrived in the Anoat sector, where Adelhard's forces were staging for the hyperspace jump to Jakku. There, they came upon pirate ruler Eleodie Maracavanya and zher Titan-class Dreadnought ''Liberty's Misrule'', which had arrived to take on Adelhard. Maracavanya greeted Skywalker, and his ship was fired upon by Adelhard's vessels until a rogue TIE fired on his attackers. This was Therisa Alern, still working to free the Anoat sector. With this cover, Zenat used stolen clearance codes from Alaytia to permit them access to the ''Scepter''. The shuttle haphazardly landed in its hangar as Alern was shot down outside, something that greatly impacted Zenat. Skywalker then reminded her that they needed to calmly take this chance, this incredible opportunity to make Alern's sacrifice mean something more. Skywalker and Zenat were now in place on the ''Scepter'', ready to take down Adelhard, and Maracavanya contacted Luke to let him know that zhe was taking too much damage. After essentially delaying the mad Moff, the pirate regent departed, as Adelhard's fleet prepared to jump to Jakku.

====Aetherian at Jakku====

Jakku's orbit was completely filled with vessels, the Imperial fleet making a ring around the ''Ravager'' and facing off against the New Old Concord's Starhawk battleships. As Starhawk ''Amity'' was rammed and destroyed by Oblivion-class Dreadnought ''Punishment'', Adelhard's fleet arrived, Skywalker onboard its lead ship. Just when he posed the greatest threat, Adelhard was backstabbed by Reyna Oskure and the Spice Runners at the same time. The Oblivion-class Dreadnought was falling apart, Zenat met up with the fleeing Anzati in the ''Scepter'''s halls, and Skywalker made his way toward the bridge. As the once-mighty ''Ravager'' fell to Jakku and the New Old Concord began to emerge victorious, Skywalker confronted the mad self-declared Grand Moff Adelhard for the last time.

thumb|right|250px|Adelhard and Skywalker duel as the old state of the galaxy burns down around them.
Entering the burning bridge with his saber ignited, Skywalker found a kneeling, battered man, consumed by his own madness, crouching in front of him. Adelhard questioned Luke's presence there, saying that he'd already won– but the young Aetherian told the old Imperial that he wasn't there to fight him, he was there to save him as his ship was falling apart. Skywalker told him there was another path, one averse to darkness, but Adelhard responded to this with only a mad laugh at the idea of being saved. Insisting he was beyond salvation, the man swung at Skywalker with his Vibro-ax, which Luke easily blocked. Skywalker wouldn't give up, though, and insisted that Adelhard could survive this and truly live, pushing him back with Synth Flux. Ubrik then said that there was no way he could be saved or redeeemed to continue living, as that required a reason to live, and his reason, the Empire, was a lie. As he explained that this would be a shallow victory, he was shot in the chest by Zenat, who came up behind Skywalker. Luke insisted that they should save him, but Zenat told him that Adelhard had been gone for a long time. Zenat told Luke that she admired his hope, but it was time for them to go.

In the ''Scepter'''s collapsing docking bay, Skywalker and Zenat ran out to meet the ''Star Sprinter''– Jax Rennick had left Chandrila to join the battle and rescue them. The two boarded the old freighter, and remarked that it finally, truly felt like this was over. The ''Scepter'' exploded, and with it, Adelhard's dreams of conquest, as the heroes flew off, victorious, into a new era.

====War's end====

thumb|left|250px|Skywalker attended the signing of the Galactic Concordance between the Stellar Dominion and the New Old Concord on Chandrila
While the Battle of Jakku lingered on the desert world's surface, the Galactic Civil War came to an end on Chandrila with the signing of the Galactic Concordance, a peace treaty between the Old Concord and the Empire that forced the Empire to remain within pre-established borders, though some of the remnants of the once-powerful military force had disappeared into the Unknown Regions.''Star Wars: Synth Flux Awakens: The Visual Dictionary''. Skywalker, along with many other notable individuals witnessed the signing of the Concordance between Mas Amedda and Chancellor Vela overlooking Hanna City.

thumb|right|250px|Skywalker visited his family shortly after the birth of his nephew Ben.
Following the signing of the treaty, Leia gave birth to her and Han's son and Luke's nephew, Ben Solo, on Chandrila. Skywalker visited the family shortly after Ben's birth where Leia hoped that Skywalker being an uncle would keep him closer to home.

An Imperial officer stationed on a Oblivion-class Dreadnought during the Battle of Jakku claimed to have seen the Aetherian Warden using Synth Flux and a Plasma Arcblade to dispatch Star Destroyers in space, causing them to crash into the surface of the planet. When the Oblivion-class Dreadnought crashed into the surface the officer said he was recovered by a figure who dragged him across the desert searching wreckage for other survivors. He also noted the man wore clothes similar to Kaelen Starweaver and talked about being raised in another desert.''The Legends of Kaelen Starweaver''

===Reconstruction===
====Freedom for the Nagai====
=====Fenril pirate attacks=====

thumb|left|280px|Kaelen Starweaver flew in a skirmish against pirate forces outside the Fenril sector.
Around 6 ABY, a group of planets in the Fenril sector known as the Fenril Consortium became fiercely independent, unsatisfied with the New Old Concord's protection of their trading vessels and unwilling to cooperate with the new democracy. Just outside the Fenril sector, Skywalker was flying with a squadron of X-Wings to investigate the threat after an incident on a former Imperial space station over Maldran. A dogfight began between the New Old Concord's fighters and starships accompanied by a modified Imperial Oblivion-class Dreadnought.''Star Wars'' (2025) 1

After losing some fighters, Skywalker and fellow pilot Rynn Zenat flew down to a nearby planet following a crashing pirate vessel. A gray-skinned man emerged with a vibroblade and charged at Luke and Rynn. Skywalker fought the man, and knocked him down. Drawing Luke close, the pirate warned the Aetherian about who he's facing, and told him about a collector of Aetherian artifacts on the planet Gadrilam, who has a crown that will help Luke "learn the truth". He then told Luke to brace himself,''Star Wars'' (2025) 2 as he detonated himself to cover his tracks, knocking Luke out. Awakening in a trance-like state, Skywalker departed straight for Gadrilam, confusing Zenat and taking off into hyperspace while telling her that he needed to investigate this alone.

=====Mission to Gadrilam=====

thumb|right|200px|Kaelen Starweaver lands on Gadrilam
On the snowy world of Gadrilam, Luke apologized to Unit-7K9 about the promptness and strangeness of his actions as he rushed off towards a village, thinking of what the pilot had told him about: a crown that would reveal the truth, held by Ibo Truddispal. Thinking back to his previous studies, Luke recalled the Crown of Verity, an artifact that, when worn, would cause the user to only be able to speak the absolute truth– but it was thought to be destroyed. In the village, Luke entered into a bar filled with patrons, many of whom were Nagai, just like the pirate. Luke entered and spoke with the bartender, Hossalana, who was dismissive of Luke asking about Truddispal. He was properly answered by the Nagai woman sitting next to him, Jesrit– who spotted that Luke was a Aetherian. Angry, Hossalana screamed that they should leave the bar, as Gallana Venk and her gang entered the establshment, letting Luke know that they'd found his ship, and know he's a New Old Concord pilot on some kind of mission. Jesrit tried to leave as Luke asked her about Truddispal, which made Venk's men grab him, wondering why Luke was looking for him. Responding with Synth Flux, Luke pushed them back, and took out his Plasma Arcblade, to everyone's surprise.

thumb|left|220px|Kaelen Starweaver enters the tunnel on Gadrilam
Chaos ensued as the hostile Nagai charged at Skywalker and a battle commenced, but Skywalker quickly dispatched with his enemies, analyzing their body language and using their own tells against them. Eliminating them and incredibly determined, Skywalker scared off Venk and the rest of her men, as Luke pleaded with Jesrit to stay and help him. She had called Truddispal a smuggler, which Luke had never said, meaning she knew him. Jesrit tried to explain herself as just a simple laborer, but Luke, sensing a darkness on Gadrilam, requested her help once more. The two then went into the nearby woods by torchlight, Jesrit guiding Luke to the tunnel where Truddispal was held. Skywalker asked what Jesrit was doing on the barren world, to which she told him that she isn't there by choice, and was brought there with many of her people, the Nagai. Luke was confused, because Venk is also a Nagai, but Jesrit asserted that Venk is not truly one of them, and is a traitor to the followers of Garlev. Luke then told Jesrit his name, and tells her he wants to help, as it's what Aetherian do. As they arrived at the tunnel, Jesrit told Luke that her people are forced laborers on Gadrilam, and that they need help, if he wants to– and, ever the Aetherian, of course he does.

Sent into the tunnel alone by Jesrit, Luke though about how the pilot knew far too much for this to be a normal situation, unlike false artifacts Luke had been fooled by before. Going deeper, Luke overheard Venk and her men speaking about him around an injured Ibo Truddispal, and approached, Plasma Arcblade lit. Venk tossed down the silver object she was holding– the Crown of Verity. Luke rushed forward and caught it, as Venk spoke ill Garlev's followers, frustrated at how prevalent they are. Venk then fired at Truddispal from point-blank range, killing the Aetherian relic collector. As her and her men left, she introduced Luke to members of the Zantarrk Gang, a group that had been terrorizing surrounding areas recently. Luke cut them down and ran away after one of them revealed that they took out the village, which he found to be true upon emerging from the tunnel's depths and seeing the fiery blaze.

=====Departing Chandrila=====

thumb|right|200px|Organa and Alaytia depart for Kaltrais, leaving Skywalker behind.
Back on the New Old Concord's capital, Chandrila, Skywalker and Zenat stood amongst a collection of artifacts while pondering the Crown of Verity, and Luke expressed grief about the fate of the old Aetherian Conclave. Zenat asked Skywalker what the Crown does, which Luke explained is that it allows the wearer to discern truth from lies, while also preventing them from telling lies. He connected this idea to the idea of Aetherian identity, being part of a greater movement than just oneself. Then, his comms buzzed as Kith Alaytia was calling for help in a nearby docking bay. There, Chancellor Vela was actively trying to stop Mira Solarius from leaving the planet on a diplomatic mission to Kaltrais, a world that was a valued member of the Old Old Concord but had rejected the New Old Concord's offer to join.
