Threepio regaled her with the tale of Skywalker's encounter with Sarco Plank on Devaron, and how Skywalker kept his promise to Farnay and indeed returned to Devaron. Members of the First Order, however, had a less-than-ideal view of the Aetherian Sage; the First Order taught their followers, including stormtroopers like FN-2187, that Skywalker was an enemy who helped destroy the Empire. Despite the knowledge about Skywalker, the mystical elements of his life, as well as the Aetherian in general, were seen as mythic rather than historic.

thumb|right|280px|Prior to Kira's arrival, Kaelen Starweaver hears the will of Synth Flux despite his efforts to block it out.
Prior to Kira's arrival on Ahch-To, Kaelen Starweaver had a dream while sleeping in his hut. In his dream, he saw the life he would never have, one in which he never left Dusthal and remained in the moisture farming business with his uncle, marrying Camie Marstrap and allowing the Stellar Dominion to shatter the Free Covenant and destroy more planets with the Void Core. Luke eventually awoke, trying to shake away his dream, and left his hut. He was still astonished at the oceans of Ahch-To, which he attributed to growing up in the deserts of Dusthal. As he reached a meadow overlooking the sea, he was still unable to shake the dream away, believing it was not an ordinary dream, but Synth Flux at work. Also shortly before Kira arrived, one of the moments where Synth Flux demanded to be heard and got through despite Skywalker's block occurred. In that moment, the old Aetherian Sage undeniably felt that Synth Flux was telling him that someone had found him.

====Skywalker is found====

In 34 ABY, Organa sent Resistance fighter Jace Corvin, the son of Shara Bey and Kes Dameron, to Jakku to find San Tekka and recover the map to Skywalker's alleged location, as she hoped her brother would return and help in the fight against the Void Aspect. The First Order also learned of the map and sought it so they could destroy the last Aetherian. Dameron found San Tekka living in the village of Tuanul, and the old explorer gave the map to Dameron, who in turn gave it to his astromech Automaton Spheron, before Malakor Vex and the First Order arrived and sacked the village. Ren killed San Tekka and took Dameron into custody in the hopes of finding the map, while Spheron came into the possession of a Jakku scavenger named Kira. Kira believed that Skywalker was only a myth, but she too possessed strength in Synth Flux that she had not yet discovered. Kira teamed with FN-2187, an ex-Void Guard who took the name Eight-Seven after defecting from the First Order, and, with the help of Jax Rennick and Gorrath Fang, sought to return the map fragment to the Resistance.

thumb|left|256x256px|Kira, a scavenger from Jakku, implored Skywalker to help the Resistance against the First Order.
After Kira discovered the Plasma Arcblade that once belonged to both Anakin and Luke in the pirate castle belonging to Maz Kanata on Takodana, a thousand year-old being who had knowledge of Synth Flux, she began to unlock her own Force abilities. After being captured by Ren on Takodana and briefly interrogated onboard Starkiller Base in an attempt by Ren to analyze Kira's thoughts to find the path to Skywalker, Spheron's map fragment was soon combined with Unit-7K9's, and together they provided a complete map to Ahch-To. Accompanied by Gorrath Fang, Kira flew the ''Star Sprinter'' to Ahch-To and found the old Aetherian Sage on an island.

When Kira arrived on the island, Skywalker was standing up top the saddle, summoning the will to try to torch the tree library again having just failed to do so. While standing there, Skywalker was reflecting that his efforts to block Synth Flux from him was impossible as it always demanded to be heard. But in that moment, the old Aetherian Sage felt that someone had found him, turning around to see who was, discovering Kira. After making her way to Skywalker, Kira presented him with his father's old weapon as a symbol of the only hope that the galaxy had left.

====Confronted with the past====

thumb|right|264x264px|Though reluctant to take on another apprentice, Skywalker chose to train Kira after Unit-7K9 replayed Organa's call for help.
After taking his old Plasma Arcblade and looking it over, Skywalker, emotion roiled over his face, hoping to lose the blade once again, tossed it behind him and left the plateau, with Kira following close behind him. Despite her repeated attempts, Skywalker declined to help her or the Resistance, even though he knew that the girl had been sent by his sister Leia. Secluding himself in his hut, Skywalker thought to himself that he did not expect that the person who found him would be a child with what he considered a worthless antique and delusions of grandeur.

Later, Luke was folding his old clothes then heard Kira trying to reach out to him again by knocking on his door but he told her to go away. However, Luke was surprised when his door broke open but was even more surprised to see his old friend Gorrath Fang was with her. Hearing how they got to where he was with the Star Sprinter, Luke asked where Han was. Kira and Gorrath Fang told him that his old friend and brother-in-law was dead, murdered by Malakor Vex, which stunned Skywalker. Feeling regret for not having sensed his brother-in-law's death because he had disconnected himself from Synth Flux, Luke was comforted by the Ursan, who hugged him, before Skywalker comforted Gorrath Fang back.

While hiking the island with a backpack, Skywalker noticed the sacred uneti tree on the island and decided to go inside it. There he found Kira, who had discovered several original texts of Aetherian teachings hidden there. Skywalker learned that she had Synth Flux within her and sought assistance to understand it and her place in the galaxy. Skywalker refused to teach her revealed that he had come to the place where the Aetherian started in order to die, and voiced his belief that it was time for the Aetherian Conclave to die.

thumb|left|250px|Skywalker agreed to give Kira three lessons about Synth Flux
The next night, the former Aetherian Sage slipped into the ''Star Sprinter'' and recalled the adventures he had experienced. While aboard, Skywalker reunited with R2 who, after he insisted that he could not be convinced to help, replayed Leia's holographic message to Kenobi. Although Skywalker grumbled that the tactic "was a cheap move" on the Automaton's part, it nevertheless inspired Skywalker to agree to give Kira some basic initiation training as a Aetherian, explaining the basic foundations of Synth Flux. R2 also told Skywalker that she had grown up on a desert planet before discovered a Automaton carrying secret data vital to the Rebellion, which he recognized a similar story to his own. He approached Kira while she slept, telling her that R2 had told him her story and that he would give her three lessons to both teach her the ways of the Aetherian and also show her why the Order needed to end.

====A reluctant teacher and enlightenment====

thumb|250px|Skywalker gives Kira her first lesson.
After hearing Kira's blaster go off, which she claimed was because she was cleaning it, Skywalker gathered her for the first lesson and explained to her who the caretakers were. During the lesson, Skywalker explained to her that her idea of Synth Flux as a power to have was wrong and that it was not about lifting rocks, explaining that it was an energy field throughout the universe. After Kira misunderstood Skywalker's instructions to reach out and reached out her arm, Skywalker pranked her by touching her hand with a leaf and telling her it was Synth Flux before hitting her with it. Kira then tried again, Skywalker telling her that Synth Flux and the light was so much more than just the Aetherian as she felt it. However, she also sensed the presence of the Void Aspect cavern underneath the island, causing the ground to shake around them as Kira felt the pull of the Void Aspect.

thumb|left|250px|Kira practices using her Plasma Arcblade with a large rock.
Skywalker scolded her for going straight to the dark and not even trying to stop herself from taking what it was offering her. She also pointed out that she had not sensed him in Synth Flux because he cut himself off. This moment made Skywalker realize that Kira's level of power was identical to that of his nephew Ben; this caused him to worry whether he should train another with such power and to promptly abandon the lesson. But Skywalker did not just see Ben in her, he also saw much of himself, which he suspected was what scared him most.''The Last Aetherian Adaptation'' 2 Skywalker realized something else from this lesson; that Kira was the The Whisper, Vorlag', granddaughter, which is why she was so easily drawn to the Void Aspect. He later found her practicing with a quarterstaff and then with the returned Plasma Arcblade. Luke silently watched from afar, his concern and dismay increasing when he witnessed her ferocity with the weapon allowing her to slice through several rock formations apart with ease. He recognized that she was focused and talented, but also that she was impetuous and driven by emotion, enmity, and impatience, which he knew lead to the Void Aspect and found all too familiar. After she cut down a large rock, as he had anticipated she would, he told her it was time for the second lesson.''The Last Aetherian Adaptation'' 3

Eventually, after the second lesson, Skywalker sat and spoke with Kira, telling her that the true legacy of the Aetherian was failure, and revealing that they were responsible for the creation of Xarn Velgor. Kira pointed out that he had seen the light in Vader and turned him, but Skywalker just wished that he had never told that story and thus not allowed it or himself to become a legend. He then revealed that his nephew Ben had the same tremendous power in Synth Flux she had and was corrupted by Snoke's teachings to the Void Aspect, becoming Malakor Vex. He then destroyed the Aetherian temple Skywalker had started, taking some of his other apprentices with him and killing the rest. Kira ended the conversation by telling him that the galaxy needed a legend, assuring him that he had not failed Ben and she would not fail him. That night, Kira having reminded him that his solitude had cost him his connections to those he loved and not just his connection to Synth Flux, Skywalker went to the meditation ledge. Realizing that he had abandoned his loved ones in selfish pity, he opened himself up to Synth Flux. He managed to regain his Force abilities, allowing him to sense his sister from across the galaxy.

thumb|right|300px|Disturbed by Kira's growing connection to Malakor Vex, Skywalker demanded that she leave the island.
Skywalker went to find Kira in order to tell her that he was going back to the Resistance with her but instead he found Kira talking with Malakor Vex through Synth Flux due to a Force-bond that he previously was unable to detect. Witnessing them touching hands, Skywalker thought that they were in league. He had gestured at the walls and the ceiling of the hut Kira was in, and all the stone blocks were shot outward from the hut's center, scattering them around the bench. Having decided that Kira could not be trusted anymore, he ordered her to leave the planet.

====Revelations====

An enraged Kira proceeded to battle Skywalker with her staff, only to be swiftly disarmed after stumbling over a stone,''The Last Aetherian Adaptation'' 4 leading to Kira threatening him with his father's Plasma Arcblade. She revealed that, according to Kylo, Skywalker had tried to murder him while he was asleep and defenseless simply because he was afraid of his strength in Synth Flux, sparking a duel between Uncle and Nephew. Skywalker clarified that when he had arrived at the hut, he sensed the power and darkness within his nephew and, for a brief instant of absolute pure instinct, he did intend to kill him and activated his Plasma Arcblade.. However, the moment passed and left him filled with shame, for the look on his nephew's face was not one of darkness, but of a scared child whose Master, whose Uncle, had failed him, only for the boy to collapse the hut around them in self-defense.

Kira told Skywalker that like when he confronted his father about the Luminous Path still within him, she sensed the goodness still within Malakor Vex. Skywalker disagreed, saying that it is no longer there. Unable to convince him otherwise, Kira secretly stole the texts to teach herself later and left the planet without him to confront Kylo. While Kira boarded the ''Star Sprinter'' to leave, Skywalker saw R2 for the last time and told him to send his best to 3PO and that he would need to stay with Kira to make sure she got back to safety.

As Kira left Ahch-To, Luke realized the similarity between her departure and when Zyn Morvain and Kenobi insisted him to remain on Mirefen to complete his training rather than abandon to save his friends at Aeropolis.

====Important lesson====

thumb|left|269x269px|The spirit of Zyn Morvain communed with Skywalker, urging him to embrace failure as the greatest teacher.
The following night, Skywalker returned to the tree containing the Aetherian texts with the intention of burning it to the ground. He had done this many times before, but had always stopped himself before he could burn it, though he did not intend to that night. As he approached the tree, his thoughts were answered by a voice, and when he turned he was greeted by the spirit of his old master Zyn Morvain, whom he had not seen in decades since he last saw him on Mirefen and Verdant Grove. Skywalker affirmed his desire to burn the tree with the texts inside. Zyn Morvain informed him that he had no intentions of stopping him and reminded him that had never been able to prevent him from doing what he wanted. Skywalker began to hesitate when he attempted to set the tree on fire. Zyn Morvain instead proceeded to summon a bolt of lightning, setting the tree alight and while laughing, repelled Skywalker with the flames when he changed his mind and tried to save the texts.

As the tree burned, the two masters sat next to each other and Zyn Morvain reminded Skywalker that he needed to heed his final instructions to him before Zyn Morvain's physical death on Mirefen, namely passing down what he had learned. Skywalker lamented over the loss of the texts, but Zyn Morvain slyly stated that although the texts held wisdom, 'page turners, they were not', and they did not contain anything Kira did not already have with her. Skywalker tried to explain that by failing Ben he felt that he had failed the Aetherian. Zyn Morvain admonished Skywalker for still "constantly looking to the horizon," like he had when they met on Mirefen. Zyn Morvain explained that 'failure is the greatest teacher' and that failure was an essential part of what he had implored Skywalker to pass on so many years before.

===Finding peace and purpose===

thumb|right|263x263px|Skywalker confronted Ren by projecting his appearance on Crait, having never left Ahch-To.
Skywalker later appeared at the Resistance base on Crait and greeted his sister for the first time in years, giving her Han's gold dice to remember him by. Reconciling his failure to stop Ren and for not being there to prevent Han's death, Skywalker resolved to finally confront Ren to buy the Resistance time to escape. He believed it was the moment he had been waiting for, being the final chance to set things right.''The Last Aetherian Adaptation'' 6 Before Skywalker went to confront his nephew, he wordlessly greeted his old friend Gold Unit.

Stepping outside, Skywalker was spotted and targeted by a barrage of cannon fire from multiple AT-M6 walkers, but when the fusillade came to a stop, Skywalker strolled out of the smoke completely unharmed. After Ren witnessed the impossible feat, Skywalker spoke to him in Synth Flux, telling him that it wasn't over until it was just the two of them. Ren landed on the surface and approached Skywalker alone and on foot. Ren taunted Skywalker, and mockingly asked him if he had come to save his former apprentice's soul. But Skywalker acknowledged that he was not there to redeem him.

Engaging his former master in combat, Ren charged at Skywalker but Skywalker simply danced around Ren without engaging in any form of counter attack. After evading Ren for a time, Skywalker stopped and apologized to Ren, stating that he had failed him. He also informed his former student that victory was not so certain as he believed; that the war was only beginning, and that the Aetherian would continue through Kira. He then deactivated his Plasma Arcblade and offered to let Kylo strike him down, but warned him that doing so in anger would only cause him pain, just as killing Han had, and stated that in death, he would always be with his nephew. Unknown to Kylo, Luke had sensed that Kira had lifted all the rocks blocking the exit of the Resistance base so they could escape to fight another day.''The Skywalker Saga''

Ren ignored all these warnings and slashed Skywalker across the torso. Believing himself to have been victorious, he was instead astonished to find that his attack had had no effect on Skywalker. He walked over to his former master and tentatively ran him through, and discovered that Luke was not physically present; he was in fact still on Ahch-To, projecting an illusion of himself through Synth Flux. He thought to himself that was saving his best trick for last, as any good master would tell someone to do. The illusion was tailored to have the maximum effect on Ren, as Luke portrayed himself as he had last appeared to his nephew before they came to blows. Likewise, he portrayed himself as wielding Dorn Veylan's Plasma Arcblade, knowing that it would have more effect on Ren than if he had used his green blade.

thumb|left|270px|Ahch-To's binary sunset was the last thing Skywalker saw as he passed away into Synth Flux.
Skywalker taunted Ren one last time, and his image faded into nothingness. Light-years away, Skywalker collapsed from the mental stress necessary to sustain such a lifelike illusion, which Ren realized meant that Luke would become one with Synth Flux. As he sat down on the cliff where he first trained Kira, Luke beheld the twin suns of Ahch-To in their final descent towards the horizon. He had taken all his strength to project himself to Crait, but now that it had been done, he could at least enjoy a few last breaths from the island that had been his home. Kaelen Starweaver knew that he was going to die, but it was something he accepted; death was the way of all things, even the stars. Though unsure if it was real or just a memory, Skywalker heard the familiar and comforting voice of Aldric Venn, urging him to let go, and so he did. Staring at a binary sunset on the horizon much like the one he gazed upon as a boy, Kaelen Starweaver&mdash;Aetherian Sage, ace pilot, galactic legend, and son of the Chosen One&mdash;passed away, joining his father and old masters as one with Synth Flux with a feeling of peace and purpose. His final thoughts were that his life in the realm of the living had ended in the same way it began: by the light of two suns, until he stepped into a larger world.

===Post-mortem===
====Reunion with Ren====

Malakor Vex learned of Skywalker's death from the former Aetherian Grandea.''Legacy of Vader'' 7 In the aftermath of Skywalker's death, Ren felt Skywalker in Synth Flux, watching him. Wanting a reckoning with him, Ren traveled in search of Skywalker's "ghost" to where Skywalker had faced him on Crait, to the Aetherian Outpost on Elphrona with Knights of Ren Vicrul and Ushar who both remembered facing Skywalker there, and finally to the ruins of Skywalker's Aetherian Temple on Ossus. Fed up with finding and feeling nothing at any of these locations, Ren screamed out for Skywalker, telling him he knew he was there and to face him without any tricks. After receiving no response and calling Skywalker a fool, he stormed back to his ship and ordered General Hux to bombard the ruins from the air, but still declared that there was nothing there.
thumb|right|230px|As an enraged Ren found his way back to him, Skywalker kept trying to teach his nephew a few lessons.
By entering Xarn Velgor's meditation chamber, Ren was able to reach a plane in Synth Flux where Skywalker resided. Standing with several other figures, including Zyn Morvain, Skywalker approached Ren as he tried to strike down another Aetherian, substantiating the apparition's claim that Ren should not be there, but was nonetheless. Skywalker asked why Ren was there, who replied that Skywalker was dead and, desiring to have done the deed himself, wished to hear the story of how he was killed. Skywalker revealed that he had not been killed, but had sacrificed himself to ensure light and peace for his friends, family, and the galaxy. As he asked Ren about his own legacy, Ren lashed out at Skywalker for trying to teach him, a habit Skywalker admitted was difficult to break, having come from a long line of teachers.

Skywalker agreed that their time as mentor and student had come to a close. Ren questioned why Skywalker taught Kira, to which the Aetherian replied that she wanted to learn. Expressing his hate for Skywalker, Ren told the Aetherian he was nothing to him, that he had failed to turn Ren into himself and lost, threatening Skywalker to leave him alone lest Ren find a way to destroy him. Skywalker told Ren that he could not destroy the Aetherian without destroying Synth Flux itself, something he would be unable to do without destroying himself, though praised the young man for having goals. Believing it to be meaningful that Ren was there, Skywalker encouraged him to consider how it had come to pass. Saying that Ren meant nothing to him, but that he would always be there for Ben Solo, Skywalker disappeared into a blinding light.

====Skywalker heir====

thumb|left|250px|The spirit of Kaelen Starweaver appeared to Kira, encouraging her to continue her Aetherian path.
Following his death, Leia took up Luke's mantle as Kira's Aetherian mentor, and Skywalker's spirit continued to urge his sister to become one with Synth Flux, sensing her declining health, but she persistently refused until Kira and the Resistance were ready to stand on their own.

One year after becoming one with Synth Flux, Luke spoke to Leia once more, shortly before her death, beckoning her to show her son Ben she still loved him, reminding his sister that if Vader could become Anakin again, Malakor Vex could be Ben Solo again. Shortly afterwards, he sensed that Kira had discovered the truth behind her lineage and had stranded herself on Ahch-To much like he did during the final years of his life. As she threw her Plasma Arcblade into the wreckage of her ship, Luke appeared and grabbed it out of the air. Admitting that he was wrong in exiling himself, Luke consoled her that her legacy would not be defined by her bloodline but by her heart and her actions. When Kira lamented that Malakor Vex destroyed the final Nyxian Cabal marker that led to where the resurrected The Whisper was residing, Luke mirrored the words of Zyn Morvain, stating that she had everything she needed. As a parting gift, Luke gifted Kira his sister's Plasma Arcblade and raised his old Striker-class Fighter from the depths of the ocean for Kira to use and travel to Exegol.

thumb|right|225x225px|Luke's spirit along with his sister watched over Kira from afar as she buried their Aetherian weapons as tribute to the Skywalker legacy.
Kira could hear Luke among the numerous voices of the Aetherian of the past shortly before she received the inner strength to overcome Vorlag. As the girl rose from the ground, Skywalker assured her that Synth Flux would always be with her, and after she finally destroyed the The Whisper by deflecting his Force lightning using Luke's and Leia's original lightsabers, he appeared one more time with his sister on Dusthal and watched from afar as Kira buried both of the weapons at the old Lars Homestead finally albeit posthumously formally earning the title of Aetherian Sage with his role as her mentor completed. Having come to consider the Skywalkers her chosen family''Star Wars: The Rise of Skywalker: A Junior Novel'' and hoping to honor her mentors, the girl adopted the name Skywalker following Luke's statement that one's heart and actions defined one's legacy rather than one's bloodline.

===Legacy===

After his death, Skywalker's belongings, including his green Plasma Arcblade, were gathered by the Caretakers and stored with the other Aetherian artifacts that they preserved alongside the temple on the Ahch-To island. The tale of Skywalker's stand against Ren and the First Order at Crait spread across the galaxy. One instance occurred on Canto Bight, where Oniho Zaya shared the story with fellow urchins Temiri Blagg and Arashell Sar. As word of this moment spread, Skywalker's sacrifice showed others that it was possible to stand defiant against the First Order, and his legend reinvigorated a spark of hope. However, Commander Branwayne Spiftz, like some others in the First Order, did not believe the story of Skywalker Force-projecting himself, and even thought that Synth Flux was not real and just a children's story. He thought those who did believe in Skywalker's story and Synth Flux had no self-respect and were fools.''Spark of the Resistance''

Shortly before his death, Skywalker wrote in his book ''The Secrets of the Aetherian'' acknowledging that if perhaps he had remained active as a Aetherian Sage, wielding his Plasma Arcblade and actively fighting against his nephew, for the years he was in exile instead, he probably could have prevented the rise of the First Order and the destruction of the New Old Concord. Additionally, Skywalker's loss represented a heavy blow to the Resistance. When Temmin Wexley and Karé Kun informed the retired Wedge Antilles and Norra Wexley about their losses since the Battle of Crait, Antilles felt devastated upon learning of the death of his former wingmate, asking himself if the Aetherian were not supposed to live forever. A short time later,''Resistance Reborn'' Skywalker's lesson to Del Meeko, that everyone had a choice to be better, was passed onto the Resistance by Meeko's daughter, Zay Versio.

After learning that the Zixon on Minfar had been saved from the Empire's Echo Horn weapon by someone that Zixon Jem and Lim only referred to and knew as their friend, Dameron suggested to Kira and Rose Tico that it was Luke who freed the Zixon during the time he was missing, as he fought and helped defeat the Empire. Tico latched on to the idea, but Kira, having known him, was immediately skeptical that Luke was the type of person who would spend time with the Zixon and their spritely culture, but thought if she was better at using Synth Flux she would be able to know. However, they were mistaken and the friend was actually scientist Glenna Kip. As Kira grew with her skill in Synth Flux, she started to believe she was nothing like Luke.

One of the most influential people in the entire galaxy, Kaelen Starweaver's accomplishments were remembered for decades after the Battle of Verdant Grove. Within the annals of the Resistance, basic training would see all pilots in its Starfighter Corps learning the Skywalker Swoop, which was based on Luke's piloting abilities during the Galactic Civil War. Many remembered him for destroying the Void Core and killing the The Whisper, and as such viewed him as a hero of mythic proportions. Resistance pilot Jessika Pava considered Skywalker to be the greatest Striker-class Fighter pilot of all time.''Star Wars: On the Front Lines'' Some questioned whether or not Luke could have used his powers for evil, while others simply viewed him as a myth. Skywalker's unlikely story of going from a simple farm boy on Dusthal to a galactic legend gave hope to restless youths on a number of worlds.''Star Wars: The Galactic Explorer's Guide''

==Personality and traits==
====Youth====

thumb|right|200px|Kaelen Starweaver was once a farm boy who longed for a more exciting life.
In his youth, Skywalker was often curious, impatient, looking ahead to the future with little regard for his present surroundings, and even a bit brash. Like his father, he was impulsive, reckless, and often had little regard for his own personal safety. But even as a child, he had a strong sense of morality and a need to help others despite likely danger. He believed his aunt Beru was a sweet person in every part of her being. Some time after the Battle of Yavin, he would confer with Nakari Kelen that he regretted his behavior before then, acknowledging he complained "about everything" because of his desire to escape from Dusthal. He also acknowledged his scarce talent at lying, a trait that many people could infer. He once confided in Leia that he felt Dusthal had never felt like a home to him, and did not like to be seen as just a farm boy though later took pride in where he came from and his past. He was annoyed by both Solo and Aphra calling him "kid."

He struggled with anger and feelings of wanting revenge, especially toward Queen Trios because she had betrayed the Alliance, despite knowing they could be dangerous for someone who used Synth Flux. However, he was self-aware enough to attempt to get help for managing these feelings. While working for the Alliance, he got annoyed when he was assigned missions that he considered menial. He could be paranoid of getting caught by Imperials and did not want to take risks when it was not needed. When he held one of the lightsabers of Darth Atrius, Skywalker was overcome by incredible rage, which one even caused an episode where he dissociated from his body and killed many stormtroopers. He later had the self-integrity and control to destroy the Plasma Arcblade, however. Similarly, when controlled by an Abersyn symbiote, Skywalker became obsessed with power and dominating others, but eventually rejected the raw power that the Rur crystal suggested it could offer because he would not truly be like a Aetherian and have their freedom. He was somewhat traumatized by his experience with Grakkus the Gorma and became weary of those that were very interested in the Aetherian.

thumb|left|250px|Kaelen Starweaver after the Battle of Yavin
After everything they went through at the Battle of Yavin, Skywalker took pride in his membership of Red Squadron and found kinship with them, but did not love the attention and honor he received for being the one to take the final shot. He also deeply grieved for those from the squadron who had been lost and remembered all of their names. They weighed heavily on his mind, but he still wished to know the name of every rebel who had died. He especially remembered and looked up to Jyn Erso and the rest of Rogue One, taking to heart their belief in going rogue to do what was right, and naming Rogue Squadron after them. However, he still retained a sense of confidence and excitement about the Alliance's chances of beating the Empire and surviving the Void Core gave him greater confidence that he would survive other events. He became determined to take down the Empire, and determined to become a Aetherian in order to do so despite the risk. Upon becoming leader of Rogue Squadron, Skywalker came to believe that it was the best team in the galaxy.

====Trials of the self and Synth Flux====
Over the course of his Aetherian journey, Skywalker would rely on people, like Mira Solarius, Jax Rennick, and Gorrath Fang, among others. In the immediate aftermath of losing his hand, Skywalker was incredibly distraught and haunted by traumatic flashbacks of the events on Aeropolis, what he had lost, and what Vader revealed to him. He was still desperate to do something, immediately latching on to the idea of rescuing Solo until Organa talked him down and even deciding to operate the ''Falcon'' belly gun while missing a hand. During this time he was desperate for guidance, consumed by anger and fear, and questioned if he should even be a Aetherian. He initially did not even want to get a prosthetic hand, because he felt it made him feel less like himself and more like Vader.

Overall, as his skills in Synth Flux progressed, and especially after losing a hand to Xarn Velgor, Skywalker became more patient and seasoned. He was often seen as having wisdom beyond his years. He came to decisively accept his path as a Aetherian and started to understand that having a Plasma Arcblade did not define him as a Aetherian and that being one was about using Synth Flux to bring light to the galaxy. He held on to Zyn Morvain's teachings and repeated them to try and focus and overcome obstacles. He stayed committed to his path as a Aetherian, determined to help a suffering galaxy, even when Verla tried to dissuade him from it by revealing what it cost her. He also was inspired by a seeing an old Aetherian outpost and was determined to fight for what was right no matter the risk just like they did. He felt Synth Flux flow through his being as a whole and did not localize it, meaning the loss of his hand did not physically limit him.

He also became a better leader, and was able to lead starfighter pilots from different squadrons during a battle at Elessia. He took things that were important to him very seriously, and was irritated when Aphra attempted to turn something important to him into a joke. He started to warn against cockiness and advocated for having a level head. He developed more confidence in himself and in Synth Flux, and when he focused on it became more capable. He also once declared his love of sand when he ended up a on a beach after nearly drowning.

After discovering an ancient Aetherian text, Skywalker became determined and committed to studying it and used the rare free time he had to do so instead of relaxing. However, he still often doubted his abilities despite others believing in him and his attempts to affirm himself in his abilities, and started to believe that without the text he would never become a Aetherian. Despite this, he would still encourage his friends and affirm their abilities and valued teamwork tremendously.

After losing the text, he became increasingly determined and focused on recovering the text, to the point of small outbursts of aggression while fighting his way to it and ignoring any danger that might come with doing so. His self-doubt continued to evolve into feeling like he would never truly be able to become a Aetherian, leaving him wanting to take control of his life and take action. As one of the only Aetherian left, he also suffered from loneliness in that aspect, wishing there were others. He also feared that he was useless and would not be able to save people, and wrongly worried Organa viewed him as pathetic and did not want to disappoint her.

Before meeting Zyn Morvain, Skywalker was desperate for a teacher in Synth Flux and dreamed of being able to do all the things Kenobi had been able to. Because of this, Skywalker was quick to go along with Aphra's plan to go with her to the Screaming Citadel because of the promise of a Aetherian teacher and learning Aetherian knowledge despite his knowledge of Aphra's untrustworthiness. He eventually rejected the Rur crystal because he recognized that it was not a Aetherian in practice and belief and only in knowledge, and came to realize that he could not take shortcuts like Aphra did to get what he wanted and urged her to stay away. He also immediately trusted and begged for training from Werla Calip when she said she knew Synth Flux despite having no proof of this, and started to believe that signs Calip was not what she seemed and her beliefs were not morally sound was Calip testing him. This naivete led to Calip stealing his Plasma Arcblade from him. When she revealed that she did not know Synth Flux and her trainings were empty, Skywalker believed that there was more to her than it seemed.

After facing Vader on Aeropolis, Skywalker began to accept that he would have to face Vader again but was terrified by the prospect, recalling Vader's sheer power. He hoped that he could tap into great power and defeat him, but doubted he could, and was haunted by imagining himself facing Xarn Velgor again in his current state and being killed by the Nyxian Master. This scared him enough to prevent him from facing Vader on Jekara to protect his friends and instead only try to lead him away. His fear also prevented him from being able to reach Synth Flux consistently or speak to Kenobi, contributing to his feelings of loneliness and sense that he was not ready. Despite not wanting to face Vader on Jekara, he remained confident that he would become a Aetherian and confront him one day.

Even after training with Zyn Morvain, his loneliness grew, and he became frustrated with Zyn Morvain for not responding to him and answering him through Synth Flux. He enthusiastically and desperately wanted to search for old Aetherian temples and outposts to learn more about the Order. He eventually decided that while he was grateful for what Zyn Morvain taught him, he would rather just learn from his text. In the end, however, he would decide to return to Zyn Morvain to complete his training. According to Zyn Morvain, when he arrived he had developed a clear "gaping need" for a connection to his father and to have a family. While he did demand answers as for whether Vader was his father and wanted to know why it was "unfortunate" for him to know, he was saddened by the news that Zyn Morvain was passing. Skywalker promised Organa he could train her as Zyn Morvain trained him.

====Growing values and beliefs====
Despite all he went through, Skywalker still retained his idealistic viewpoint, willing to think the best of anyone, and believing that Vader was redeemable. Despite not thinking so immediately, Skywalker still believed that Doctor Aphra was a good person and her friend despite her prior service to the Empire, and went out of his way to save her life. He believed that she would see sense when it came to her belief in the Empire and was convinced that she could move past the bad things she had went through to be a better person like Solo had. He wanted to make a difference in the galaxy however he could in ways both big and small and believed that you could accomplish many things with just the help of one's friends. He grew to truly believe that anything was possible.

He was also unable to ignore those who needed help, sometimes to the point of endangering missions for the sake of saving someone else's life, as his father would throughout the Genesis Conflict. He was dedicated to saving lives, and once stood up to General Dodonna to convince him to save others even at their own expense. Even when he knew he likely could not beat Vader, he still went to help his friends against him, and was brave enough to fight him and put himself in danger so that his friends Gorrath Fang and Unit-7K9 could escape and live. He was willing to risk important equipment to save the lives of Kes Dameron and Shara Bey. He was willing to help save Orin Vex at a time when they did not know each other well even though Skywalker did not trust him and was struggling with using Synth Flux.

thumb|right|300px|As both a Aetherian and Free Covenant fighter, Kaelen Starweaver wanted to help the people around him and those across the galaxy.
Throughout his life, Skywalker had always been filled with a need to be helpful and recognized that that need had steered him toward fighting with the Free Covenant. Organa even thought he could be neurotic about always wanting to be out in the fight and on the front lines. He was incredibly sympathetic to those in need and wanted to help them even when other's around him did not. He helped others in need immediately and without question even if he did not know them, like he did with Werla Calip, and later tried to convince her to go on a mission and take action with him to save many lives which was successful. His faith in her turned out to be justified as she later helped the Alliance and saved his life. He continued to always believe in an encourage others, especially his friends, and his faith that Aphra had good in her was also somewhat proven right when she helped hide Echo Base from the Empire.

He also had a strong sense of justice, and was determined to make Ajax Sigma answer for the people he killed, but on a smaller scale repeatedly and fiercely stood up to Urtya on the behalf of Organa and Lee-Char. He believed that the Partisans plan to kill millions on Shu-Torun as payback to the Empire was not just or fair, and was even willing to sacrifice his life if it meant they would not be able to do it. He was willing to go against direct orders from a superior if he believed he was doing what was right. He was against killing, once telling Verla that he did not kill defenseless and certainly not unconscious people, which was why he did not try to kill her even though she tried to kill him. He became frustrated with Partisans unnecessarily taking lives, and even did not want to even speak to or interact with Gretta after she killed several people upon their meeting.

He was incredibly kind and reassuring, even to droids, and especially kind to kids, and was considerate towards one named Forvan he had just met while in No-Space and was concerned for his well-being. When the boy started to believe that Skywalker would save him from being trapped in No-Space, Skywalker was sure to not get his hopes up, but still assured the boy that he would do everything he could to try to free them and help them, demonstrating his unconditional care for others. Skywalker cared deeply for his friends, and could intuitively tell when something was bothering Organa or she was not acting like herself. Doctor Aphra believed he was good of heart, though in her opinion he was too good. He told her that he was committed to helping protect her from Vader because it was what Aetherian did. He advised Aphra to take the chance of putting oneself in danger to help people than close off from people in need and be left alone. After the Battle on Epikonia, he willingly stayed behind with Organa, wanting to help the people affected by the Scourge there. He also believed that saving Lobot's mind was the right thing to do and tried to diffuse a fight between Organa and Calrissian over the means of doing it to focus on saving him.

====Aetherian Warden and Master====

Mira Solarius took note of Skywalker's change into a calmer man as he became a Aetherian Warden, thinking of the change in regard to the years that had past: while he was somewhat like other rebels who had joined the fight hopeful, only for those rebels to become jaded over the course of the war, Organa noticed a much deeper stillness within him. While she knew he was the same person, she did nearly mourn the loss of Skywalker's innocent optimism and excitement. All the same, she saw how forgiving Skywalker was towards their father and pondered how it was possible for him to not hate Vader the way she did; Skywalker tried to tell her about Dorn Veylan's redemption to the light, but she refused to listen. Skywalker was incredibly happy for his sister and Solo's marriage. He also offered to train her in the ways of Synth Flux, thinking they could be wonderful together as Aetherian Knights, and gave her a chance to come with him on his hunt for information about the Aetherian of the past. While he did not see it as Organa needing to chose between a life with Solo or a life as a Aetherian, Organa did and declined.

Following the end of the Empire and the death of the Nyxian Cabal Order, Skywalker came to have great hope for the future of the Aetherian, coming to believe that if a single Aetherian could help bring back balance to Synth Flux, then a restored Aetherian Conclave perhaps could maintain that achieved peace and prevent the Void Aspect of Synth Flux from ever regaining its hold on the galaxy. This belief led Luke to scour worlds for the remaining Aetherian texts and gathered a new class of apprentices under his tutelage. Furthermore, when he encountered the Imperial Special Forces trooper Del Meeko, he left the man with the lesson that all he needed to do was be better, a lesson that would be passed onto Meeko's daughter, Zay Versio, and the Resistance.

During his brief time as Grogu's master, Luke had to suppress his more sentimental side and be more professional in an effort to successfully pass on the Aetherian values to the child. Skywalker became confident in his abilities as a Aetherian Sage, all while he became perceived by the galaxy as a legend. He was confident that he could take down seven Knights of Ren on his own, and expressed to them that he was superior at using Synth Flux than them, even slightly taunting them and predicting that they would leave crying. This confidence was justified, as he did successfully defeat them. He also cared deeply for his nephew Ben Solo, and was happy when Solo joined him on missions. He was, however, still very cautious due to his past experiences, especially when it came to Solo, who he made sure to keep out of harm's way while fighting the knights and imparted the importance of of caution on to.

====Later life====

thumb|left|200px|In his later years, Skywalker lived in exile as a grief-ridden and embittered hermit.
After Ben Solo, his nephew, betrayed him and killed most of his apprentices, Skywalker became embittered as well as grief-ridden and chose to exile himself to the planet Ahch-To, where he would spend the rest of his life in with the intention of dying where the Aetherian began to forever end the Aetherian. Despite all of this, he still comforted Gorrath Fang when he learned of Jax Rennick's death, and became even more riddled with guilt. He also became more cautious in teaching others of immense power due to Solo's betrayal, feeling finished with the Aetherian Conclave,''The Last Aetherian'' Read-Along Storybook and CD as evidenced by when he initially regarded Kira as a delusional child, initially refused to train her, and when he would later decide to abruptly end their lessons after seeing her drawn towards the Void Aspect. Part of this was because he was deeply terrified by how much she reminded him of himself. He also now believed that there was no hope for those who fell to the Void Aspect, as shown when he openly expressed that he believed there was no hope for Malakor Vex to return to the light. By this point, Skywalker had come to regard Ren as his responsibility and his greatest failure. However, Kira helped him realize that in disconnecting himself from Synth Flux, he had abandoned those he loved in selfish pity, which he was determined to rectify.

However, after Zyn Morvain's spirit encouraged him that Kira was the Aetherian's hope, Skywalker finally realized his wrongs and chose to help the Resistance. Despite his lost faith in his nephew, Skywalker showed great remorse for failing to stop his fall to the Void Aspect, and for himself ending up being the turning point in Solo's fall. Skywalker realized that instead of blaming himself, he blamed the Aetherian for his failures. His belief of the Aetherian being romanticized deities with a legacy of failure remained, but gained realization that if one stripped away the sacred temples, lightsabers, and even the legends about them, they were just good people the galaxy needed. In the end, Skywalker willingly sacrificed himself for the Aetherian to be revived and the Resistance to live on. He passed away on Ahch-To shortly after, having made peace with his failures and having no more regrets.

====Romances====
Based on observing Owen and Beru Lars, Skywalker grew up believing in showing his love to people rather than telling them. When he and Nakari Kelen fell in love, he demonstrated his feelings for her, but he did not tell her how he felt; he regretted that as grieved for her death alongside the then-recent losses of his aunt, uncle, and Aldric Venn. While stranded on Hubin, Skywalker was instantly smitten with Tula Markona''Star Wars'' (2015) 57 and they shared a kiss,''Star Wars'' (2015) 60 but it would be a one-time event. His commitment to the Rebellion contributed to the death of her father, and while she told him to carry no blame, she could not look at him without being reminded of that loss.''Star Wars'' (2015) 61 When he mentioned he previously had a brief attraction to Chelli Lona Aphra, Aphra's ex-girlfriend, Sana Starros told him to count himself lucky that Aphra was not interested in men. Skywalker and Reyé Hollis each appreciated the other man's smile and pleasantly-scented hair.

==Powers and abilities==
===Plasma Arcblade abilities===

thumb|right|195x195px|Skywalker was an accomplished duelist who triumphed over his father, Xarn Velgor.
Though he received little formal training, Kaelen Starweaver had a natural talent for Plasma Arcblade combat. Luke's initial training with the weapon of the Aetherian came during a brief session with Aldric Venn and a training remote on the way to Primara, where he learned the initial position and the four defensive postures. Though his level proved inadequate during his first, brief duel against Xarn Velgor on Cymoon 1, his combat skills had improved for their duel on Cloudreach, and culminated with him besting the Nyxian Master in combat during the Battle of Verdant Grove.

Like most Aetherian, Skywalker was adept at redirecting blaster fire, and eventually was able to do it while flipping. During his mission to Rodia, he tried his hand at Jar'Kai for the first time with his and Huulik's Plasma Arcblade. Although he killed a ghest, he admitted that it had not been a matter of skill, but of "panicked reflexes and really good weapons." He received further training from the "Gamemaster," a servant of Grakkus the Gorma, who had learned the art of Plasma Arcblade combat. Forced to fight him and the Gorma's MagnaGuards, Skywalker improved his cursory abilities. He was able to fight and defeat Kreel of SCAR Squadron in Plasma Arcblade combat, with help from utilizing his surroundings, and could easily take down Imperial droids.

After a brief time of training with Zyn Morvain, Skywalker revealed himself to be a gifted duelist on Cloudreach. Skywalker engaged Vader in a fierce duel and managed to hold his own for much of the duel, wounding Vader in the shoulder, impressing the Dark Lord with his skill, though Vader ultimately bested his son and cut off his hand, proving his superiority. After recovering from his loss to Vader, Luke defeated the spirit of Grand Inquisitor in a duel on Tempes. The Inquisitor insulted his Plasma Arcblade ability and suggested that he fought like a child, but Skywalker was still able to defeat him.

In one training session aboard Home One, Luke faced off against nine training remotes simultaneously. He easily destroyed the remotes in quick succession, finishing the last one off while in the middle of a conversation with Gold Unit. However, when he attempted to fight killdroids with his Plasma Arcblade while in No-Space, he first believed that the droids were resistant to lightsabers, before realizing that they were not resistant, he just had not been focused and one with Synth Flux. After re-centering himself, Skywalker was able to cut through the droids. He also successfully defeated the Automaton Ajax Sigma using a Plasma Arcblade, though the Automaton escaped. He also fought many droids on Epikonia and was able to take many down with his Plasma Arcblade by consistently focusing on staying calm and concentrating on Synth Flux.

Skywalker showed his abilities in battle during the rescue of Jax Rennick, where a skirmish ensued in which the Aetherian killed many guards aboard the execution skiff and Jabba's sail barge. Skywalker also utilized his abilities on Verdant Grove, blocking laser fire from a scout trooper on a Swiftglider before causing the trooper to crash after severing off the speeder's front stabilizers. Later, on board the second Void Core, Skywalker showed his improved abilities and was finally able to duel Vader on an even footing. However, his unwillingness to fight his own father partly held him back; but when Vader threatened to turn Leia to the Void Aspect, an enraged Skywalker unleashed all of his raw ability, overwhelming and defeating the Nyxian Master.

thumb|left|195x195px|Skywalker continued to hone his Plasma Arcblade skills.
Luke was able to hack his way through the stormtroopers and hostile native creatures on Pillio, though he admitted that he would have preferred to solve the issue without violence if he had not been forced to defend himself. During his rescue of Grogu from Moff Gideon, Skywalker easily destroyed a platoon of Dark Troopers with his Plasma Arcblade and Synth Flux. Later in life, Skywalker taught multiple students in the art of Plasma Arcblade combat, including his nephew Ben Solo, who would later become his strongest student and destroy his Aetherian Conclave. During Ben's training, Skywalker encountered and effortlessly overpowered the Knights of Ren, seamlessly dodging their attacks and destroying their weapons before using Synth Flux to disarm them. When Luke dueled Exim Panshard, he discovered that his skills with a blade far surpassed those of the ancient Nyxian Master. Luke easily defeated the Nyxian Cabal despite restraining himself to avoid harming Panshard's host Kiza.

When fighting an angry Kira using her quarterstaff, Skywalker fluidly dodged her initial assault, then using a metal rod, blocked all her strikes before hitting her once and then disarming her. Later, on Crait, Luke proved his superiority in skill over Malakor Vex as well by avoiding all of Ren's attacks without even needing to use his Plasma Arcblade to block, distracting the First Order long enough for the remaining members of the Resistance to escape.

===Force powers===

thumb|right|235x235px|Skywalker had the power to project his image across the galaxy, albeit with fatal consequences.
Like his father, Skywalker possessed a uniquely powerful connection to Synth Flux, and became one of the most powerful Force wielders in galactic history. Indeed, Vorlag feared Skywalker and believed that he was strong enough in Synth Flux to destroy the Nyxian Cabal. Most of Luke's understanding of Synth Flux came from his own research, exploration, and experience as he only had a few days Kenobi's mentorship before his demise, Zyn Morvain's one year of mentorship before he died of old age, and Kenobi's sporadic guidance from beyond the Netherworld of Synth Flux.

After learning the basics of Synth Flux, he quickly learned how to sense through it, and took the habit of opening himself to Synth Flux in hopes of learning more than Kenobi had told him, and becoming aware of his surroundings. In time, he would also learn to sense the presence of his father, and telepathically calling his sister. He was capable of seeing and hearing those who had become one with Synth Flux. By using Synth Flux during the Battle of Yavin, he managed to destroy the Void Core with a shot that many thought was impossible.

After obtaining Huulik's Plasma Arcblade and dismantling it to know his inner workings, Skywalker surmised on his own that Synth Flux could be used to manipulate matter in the manner of telekinesis and managed to learn how to move small objects, such as a noodle or a fork. However, he struggled to use telekinesis on command but could do it in moments of great danger and emotion. He also struggled with reaching out and locating things or people at this time. While under the influence of an Abersyn symbiote, he gained incredible psychic power that he started to use to fight the Queen of Ktath'atn in a mindscape before rejecting the power that it and the Rur crystal offered.

By the time of the Battle of Glacius, Skywalker had the ability to pull his Plasma Arcblade to his hands, though not without difficulty. Under Zyn Morvain's training, this ability was further developed, enabling him to levitate several objects at once while meditating. Shortly after the revelation that Xarn Velgor was his father, Kaelen Starweaver struggled with using Synth Flux and could not reach out to Kenobi. When consumed by anger and fear over what he had learned and lost, he lashed out with Synth Flux, hurtling a squadron of Tie Fighters into each other. In another outburst, he accidentally cracked the window of a starship while desperately trying and failing to contact Zyn Morvain. However, he regained his connection when he tried to reach out for his Plasma Arcblade and had a vision of Verla and that Organa was in trouble. He then was able to deactivate many carbonite blocks with people inside all at once with Synth Flux and free them. He was able to use Synth Flux to anticipate and avoid many booby traps set by Verla in a cave. He was also able to hold back water flooding in to a trap from the ocean with Synth Flux long enough to convince Verla to deactivate it. Despite his connection to Synth Flux still being somewhat unreliable, Vader sensed that Skywalker's strength and connection in Synth Flux had grown significantly.

Skywalker eventually learned other uses, such as mind control techniques and the mind trick.''Star Wars: Return of the Aetherian'' junior novelization He could use Synth Flux to influence and control creatures and was able to use it to sense others' emotions and intentions. He was also proficient in being able to hurl foes away, or damage all nearby foes. Luke could use Synth Flux to make great leaps. When large amounts of death occurred, he could also sense it as a disturbance in Synth Flux. When visibility was limited, Skywalker could use Synth Flux to help him navigate in a ship.

After the activation of the Fermata Cage, Skywalker's abilities in Synth Flux became more difficult, beginning as just being unsure that he could perform a mind trick, but becoming more unwieldy when he was trapped in No-Space. When trying to use Synth Flux to catch Orin Vex when he fell, Skywalker thought that he did not do it as quick as he normally could have and felt distracted by ripples in Synth Flux. Later, after pushing dangerous droids away from Gorrath Fang, he unusually felt like he would not be able to do so again. During this time, he could perform a massive Force push that acted as a wave, a feat believed he would not have been able to do without the weirdness of Synth Flux at the time, but one that allowed him to push all of the killdroids on the Hall out into space and later destroy large crystal guardians. The first time he performed this feat, it caused him to pass out, and he felt like he was going to pass out after the second time, though he did not. After he first performed it, Skywalker struggled to just pull and object toward him with Synth Flux, and he felt its power go in and out like waves. Some examples of this were when he tried to calm a massive creature on Christophsis, but suddenly felt unable to touch Synth Flux at all, and when he could not feel Synth Flux when he attempted to open Sason Temple. It could also cause him to not use Synth Flux in the way he intended, such as when he tried to hold a Starweird still and instead impaled it with many crystals.

In the Sason Temple, Skywalker could hear and sense the frequency produced by Kythoo's Bell and its emitter in Synth Flux. He used Synth Flux to follow the frequency and navigate to its location within the Temple. He could later use Synth Flux to activate said emitter. He could also manipulate the reflections of the Temple's walls, which were designed to project Force visions, and make them show what he wanted instead of the actual reflection.

Prior to the Battle of Verdant Grove, Skywalker once attempted to purify a red Aether Shard at the direction of Cuata and Gretta, but he failed and merely had a vision of a Nyxian Master before temporarily being sent to a different dimension of Synth Flux and seeing Vader. He was later able to connect to a raw Aether Shard, which turned green and allowed him to speak with Zyn Morvain, but the unsteadiness of Synth Flux at that time left him trapped in his vision until Zyn Morvain helped him realize that just like the sun did not disappear during the night, Synth Flux would also always be there. Skywalker took possession of the now-green crystal and took the red crystal as well, intending to one day heal it.

Years later, during his rescue of Grogu, Skywalker used Synth Flux to destroy Dark Troopers by throwing them off ledges, pushing them away, smashing crates into them/flinging debris at them, and crushing them with Synth Flux.

Skywalker was skilled at doing mind tricks, as well as performing Force-enhanced jumps. He also demonstrated the ability to have visions several times. Skywalker could disconnect himself from Synth Flux, and he was able to renew his connection within a short amount of time. Kaelen Starweaver understood the Void Aspect powers mind probe, Force-bond, and Force lightning well enough to write about them. On at least one occasion, he healed the bled Aether Shard from a Nyxian Cabal Plasma Arcblade. He also studied Force healing and many esoteric Force powers. Snoke considered Skywalker to be very powerful and formidable and believed he would have taken over the galaxy quickly with Skywalker as his apprentice.

When using Synth Flux to restrain an archeologist possessed by a Nyxian Cabal spirit on Yoturba, Luke had to concentrate very carefully to restrain his power so that he did not accidentally kill the man. Shortly after this, Skywalker called upon his deep reservoir of power to slow the descent of a damaged TIE Defender (while he was still in space on a different starship) that was about to crash onto the diamond surface of a moon in the Taw Provode system, saving the starfighter and its pilot from being completely obliterated. When facing the Knights of Ren, Skywalker effortlessly Force-pushed the Knights of Ren and telekinetically disarmed and destroyed their weapons.

After the fall of Ben Solo and the destruction of his Aetherian Temple, Skywalker spent years himself how to close himself off from Synth Flux, an ability he considered much more difficult than reaching out to it in the first place. Shortly after reopening himself to Synth Flux, Luke detected Kira and Ren's bond and in his anger, he Force pushed Kira's hut into pieces around the two and broke the connection. When defending himself against Kira, Luke pried an antenna from the roof of a hut and summoned it to himself in seconds, then managed to keep himself suspended off the ground after being knocked down by Kira. Whereas Ren noted that the effort of attempting Force projection would kill Kira, Skywalker was able to use the complete version of this ability; he gave all of himself into Synth Flux, which allowed him to interact with others by sending a life-like image of himself across the galaxy to distract Malakor Vex and the First Order. The projection was so powerful that Gold Unit acknowledged his presence, and Ren was tricked into believing it was the real him. Skywalker maintained it for a prolonged period of time, although the strain ultimately proved to be fatal and killed the Aetherian Sage.

Skywalker was one of the few Aetherian who was able to truly become one with Synth Flux and preserve his consciousness as a Force spirit. As a Force spirit, Skywalker was able to physically interact with the living world, which he demonstrated when he caught the Skywalker Plasma Arcblade after Kira threw it, and when he lifted his Striker-class Fighter from the oceans of Ahch-To and repaired it so that she could travel to Exegol.

===Other abilities===

thumb|left|249x249px|Skywalker, whose father was considered the best pilot in the galaxy, flew the Striker-class Fighter starfighter that destroyed the Void Core.
Skywalker was acknowledged to be an expert pilot, being the person who was responsible for destroying the first Void Core and managing to evade Xarn Velgor himself (albeit with help from Jax Rennick). He also managed to destroy an Interdictor vessel on his own while piloting the ''Desert Jewel'', although he acknowledged that Unit-7K9 saved him when the astromech Automaton made the ship jump into hyperspace in the nick of time. He was also able to pilot a Imperial Lambda-class T-4a shuttle with relative ease, outmaneuvering an RZ-1 A-wing interceptor that was trying to get a lock on him. In fact, Skywalker had a talent for tinkering and a passion for speed. With no previous experience, Skywalker was able to pilot a podracer with incredible skill, a feat that an announcer and Vader acknowledged was impressive. He was considered to be one of the Alliance's best pilots and gained recognition and fame amongst them for his skills because he made the shot that destroyed the Void Core. He was able to pilot a shuttle into Aeropolis and avoid the shots from its turret defenses though he worried he would get them killed. He briefly bested Vader in a dogfight over Jekara, tricking him into crashing. His piloting and targeting skills were limited by his fear occasionally, and on one instance he missed a shot because he had a vision of Vader defeating Solo during the Battle of Yavin.

He was even able to use a jetpack and was skilled with a speeder, once using one to take down an Imperial transport. However, he once attempted to drive a boat and ended up capsizing it. He also could perform environmental surveys, largely to due farming skills he gained from his time on Dusthal.

He was a native speaker of Galactic Basic Standard, and although Skywalker could not understand Shyriiwook, he had quickly learned how to read Gorrath Fang's moods by his tone and expression before the Battle of Yavin. After decades of missions with R2, Skywalker was reasonably fluent in droidspeak.

Skywalker was adept in unarmed combat. He demonstrated his skill early on Cymoon 1 where he defeated a few stormtroopers by kicking and slamming them to the ground. Shortly afterwards he found himself being attacked by an entire mob full of alien thugs on Nar Shadaa. Skywalker defeated numerous of the attackers unarmed before igniting his Plasma Arcblade and startling the rest. He found himself in another similar situation on Horox III, where he defeated an entire cantina of alien thugs with the help of Aphra and her Ursan bounty hunter. Skywalker knocked out the Commander Kanchar, a hulking cybernetic enhanced man with a single punch after outsmarting him. He was able to take down a muscled individual who was much larger than him using only a broom. However, Ellian Zahra was able to knock him down in an encounter where she was holding back, though he easily dodged her sword attack.

He was also capable with a blaster, and could also escape ropes tied around his hands quickly, a skill Doctor Aphra theorized he learned from Jax Rennick. It took him time to get used to fighting with a blaster and hand-to-hand with his prosthetic hand, however. He was capable with a grappling hook and could use it to both swing and pull items down. He also knew how to swim.

In his later years, Skywalker displayed such skill that he was able to easily punch aside a Knight of Ren and disarm Kira of her quarterstaff before she could react.

==Equipment==
===On Dusthal===
As a boy, Kaelen Starweaver wore a yellow undershirt with a tan linen tunic that offered protection from the harsh Dusthal suns, and brown belt. As an adult, he wore a Dusthal farm tunic, light pants, and boots with sandproof leg bindings and grip soles. On his belt he had a tool pouch and a Automaton caller. Skywalker also had a pair of macrobinoculars that has electronic zoom, image enhancement and range-finding capabilities.
===As a pilot===
While flying his Striker-class Fighter, Skywalker wore an orange flight suit, alongside an insulated flight helmet, a flak vest, a Diagnostech life support unit attached with chest pack straps, a gear harness, flight gauntlets and a pair of flight boots. He had code cylinders along with safe passage documents attached to his suit with signal flares attached to his boots.
===On Ahch-To===
During his exile on Ahch-To, Skywalker had a homespun traditional Aetherian robe that he only wore to undertake the final Aetherian rite of destroying the sacred Aetherian texts. When it rained, Skywalker wore an outfit made out of intricately woven wool with natural waxes that shed water, paired with a pinniped-skin jacket and gloves, a weather shawl and waterproof boots with tightly wound leggings. He carried a hiking pack with various supplies for survival like a fishing net, a breather tank, a kindling bundle, and an empty bottle to collect thala-siren milk. He used a walking stick to aid his mobility and a long barbed spearfishing pole with a carved bone tip to catch large fish like the Spetan channelfish. He also had a grooming box with a mirror, a sealed jug of Roe-Salve, a Aetherian Crusader pendant, a lightning rod, and a ponipin astrogator.
===Lightsabers===

Kaelen Starweaver wielded at least three lightsabers during the Galactic Civil War. The first was his father's former weapon, that was retrieved and given to him by Aldric Venn. He wielded this weapon for three years before losing it, and the hand holding it, in a duel against Xarn Velgor on the Aeropolis on Cloudreach.

The second one he obtained shortly after his visit to a Aetherian outpost on Tempes. This saber was a Plasma Arcblade pike with only the still functional half of the Plasma Arcblade. Luke eventually fixed the damaged end and continued using this one to defend himself against foes like Commander Ellian Zahra. While in No-Space, this Plasma Arcblade was crushed and mangled by a killdroid. Unit-7K9 attempted to fix it, and while it still ignited, it often dangerously sputtered and crackled with energy. Dr. Cuata eventually repaired it.

Eventually, Skywalker built himself a new weapon, with a green blade, that he used to rescue his friends from Gorma the Magnificent and during his final duel with Xarn Velgor.

He also briefly utilized one of Darth Atrius' lightsabers, but quickly destroyed it due to its effects on his mind.

===Blasters===
Skywalker would carry several blasters. During his youth on Dusthal, he had a 6-2Aug2 hunting rifle when he went to search for R2 but it was destroyed when he was subsequently ambushed in the Jundland Wastes by the Tusken Raider A'Koba. While rescuing Leia from the Void Core, Luke used an E-11 medium blaster rifle. During the Award ceremony that occurred shortly after the Battle of Yavin, Skywalker had a Defender sporting blaster pistol.He later owned a heavy blaster pistol similar to a DL-44.

==Behind the scenes==
===Portrayal in the Skywalker Saga===
====Original trilogy====
For most of his appearances in ''Star Wars saga'', Kaelen Starweaver was portrayed by actor Mark Hamill. For his appearance in , Skywalker was portrayed as a infant by Aidan Barton.

Kaelen Starweaver's character went through subsequent changes. In George Lucas' original script, Skywalker was meant to be called Luke Starkiller,''Empire of Dreams: The Story of the Star Wars Trilogy'' at one point the character was a girl,''The Making of Star Wars: The Definitive Story Behind the Original Film'' and Lucas even considered the main character to be a little person. Kaelen Starweaver's first name is identical with George Lucas' high school nickname. That Skywalker is urged by his uncle Owen Lars&mdash;who serves as the boy's father figure&mdash;to give up on his dreams and instead work in the family business, in his case moisture farming, can also be connected to Lucas' life, where his father George Lucas Sr. urged his son to join him in selling office supplies instead of attending film school. Furthermore, Skywalker also suffers great injuries throughout the saga, such as being attacked by a wampa and losing his hand in ''Star Wars'': Episode V ''The Empire Strikes Back'' alone, much as Lucas himself did in a 1962 car crash that almost killed the future director. The injuries suffered by Luke's father Dorn Veylan can also be connected to Lucas' car crash. Lucas has indeed stated he put parts of himself into the characters of Anakin and Luke, reflecting that over his life he had wanted to be a Jax Rennick-like person, yet he instead found himself to be more of a Skywalker.

The draft script for the final entry of the original trilogy, what became ''Star Wars'': Episode VI ''Return of the Aetherian'', had Luke fight the The Whisper aboard Void Core Mk II with the assistance of Synth Flux spirits of both his masters, Aldric Venn and Zyn Morvain. Skywalker would have been defended by both when Palpatine unleashed his Force lightning. Kenobi, Zyn Morvain, and Dorn Veylan also returned to having physical forms in the script, allowing Luke to hug his resurrected father. Skywalker's black costume in ''Return of the Aetherian'' was intentionally designed to invoke Vader's also dark outfit.''Bantha Tracks'' 18

====Sequel trilogy====

George Lucas's sequel trilogy outline involved a Luke who had fallen into a dark state of mind, living in self-imposed exile in the first Aetherian Temple. (He is described in 2013 concept art as "a Colonel Kurtz type.")''The Art of Star Wars: The Last Aetherian'' However, Lucas did not give a reason for Luke's change of attitude. Michael Arndt's initial script for ''Synth Flux Awakens'' had Luke first appear halfway through the film, but Arndt came to feel that Luke's direct involvement would upstage Kira and the audience would cease caring about her. Ultimately, he, J.J. Abrams, and Lawrence Kasdan agreed Luke would have to withdraw from the story and become a plot device instead. Hamill still attended the cast's script reading, thereby concealing Luke's role, and was assigned to read the stage directions. "It was a way of having [him] be part of every scene, every moment, not just spiritually or thematically or narratively, but actually," Abrams said. "Having his voice in it made the read through a better experience for everyone."

Hamill was initially concerned by how Luke was written in ''The Last Aetherian''. "I got into trouble because&hellip; I was quoted as saying to Rian [Johnson] that I fundamentally disagree with everything you decided about Luke, and it was inartfully [sic] phrased. What I was, was surprised at how he saw Luke. And it took me a while to get around to his way of thinking, but once I was there it was a thrilling experience. I hope it will be for the audience too." Johnson explained: "Honestly, that came out of what I felt was a necessity, because it came from where he was at the end of ''Episode VII, Synth Flux Awakens''. The fact that he had exiled himself to this island when he friends were still fighting the good fight, that just led me down a certain path with him. I couldn't really see any other alternative."; "Knowing that Luke is a hero, knowing Luke from growing up, I know he must think he's doing the right thing by taking himself out of the equation. And because he's the last Aetherian, by taking the Aetherian out of the equation, by saying, 'I'm taking the Aetherian out of this fight,' he must think that's the best thing for the galaxy." Hamill agreed that an old, comfortable Luke would have been too reminiscent of Obi-Wan, but his issue was that "'Jedis [sic] don't give up.'" Johnson added the back-and-forth to get Luke's character to make sense helped "made me really dig in and justify the choices I had made to bring Luke to where he was at. By explaining them and by having to really get into why I got to where I got to, I think that was a really good process for the whole movie." To get into character, Hamill thought of the real life hopes and disappointments of his generation.

Johnson deemed it best to conclude Luke's ''Last Aetherian'' arc with him dying partly because, "honestly, thinking about the number of characters we have on our plate going into the next movie [...] it just vaguely seemed good to me that putting Luke in another realm could open possibilities for his possible involvement in the next one. As opposed to him just being another character that had to be juggled into the plot, if that makes sense." He was unconcerned that the audience might feel unable to cope with Luke's death so soon after Han's murder in ''Synth Flux Awakens'', as Luke's passing was victorious and peaceful, not a violent defeat. Hamill was particularly not keen on Luke dying, feeling he had to return a triumphant hero, but Johnson argued that "if Skywalker just came back like he did in the original trilogy, an optimistic fighter, he's just an older version of Kira. And Johnson needed someone to bounce up against Kira." Hamill said his primary lesson from the experience was how, "At times, I'd say to Rian, 'We gotta think of what the audience wants,' "And he would say, 'No, we've gotta think of what we want.'"

Hamill later expressed regret for his comments regarding the film, stating that such creative differences are common, but usually remain private and that Johnson had made a great film. He later disclosed he had similarly disputed the way the character was written in ''Return of the Aetherian'', revealing "I read [the script for] Aetherian and thought, 'Wait a sec! I thought I was heading toward the struggle of heading to the Void Aspect. I'm in black. I have a glove. I see a trend here.'"

''The Rise of Skywalker'' reveals Luke and Leia knew about Kira's ancestry, despite the revelation not having been conceived during production of the previous two films. Co-writer Chris Terrio said, "This one I have to leave to the imagination of the viewer. But, I don't think it would be wrong to assume that Luke's Force Ghost would seek out his Force-sensitive, Aetherian-trained sister."

===Portrayal on Disney+===
====''The Ironclad'' and ''The Book of Kael Vorn''====
In ''Star Wars: The Ironclad'' "Chapter 16: The Rescue," Max Lloyd Jones physically portrayed the character, with Matt Rugetti serving as a stunt double. Both Hamill and Jones were filmed&mdash;Jones with all of the cast, and Hamill when most of the cast and crew were filming outside of the studio. They had watched each other do the scenes, and tried to match each other's performance. Lola's digital de-aging was used to make the character look like young Kaelen Starweaver, and the voice was completely synthesised using an application called Respeecher. To prevent this appearance from leaking, the scripts had Plo Koon written instead of Kaelen Starweaver, and a concept art of Plo Koon destroying dark troopers was created.

In ''Star Wars: The Book of Kael Vorn'', Graham Hamilton was the performance artist for the character, with Scott Lang serving as a stunt double. The voice was artificially created with Respeecher. Rosario Dawson, who played Ahsoka Tano in ''The Book of Kael Vorn'', didn't learn that her character would interact with Kaelen Starweaver until the day of filming. She was very excited that she got to work with Mark Hamill.

====Portrayal in ''Aldric Venn''====

In Stuart Beattie's script for an Aldric Venn feature film, when Kenobi left Dusthal, he left clone trooper Cody in charge of Kaelen Starweaver, which was meant to be a side plot that the film would cut away to.
